::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Khuddakanikāye

## Therāpadānapāḷi

#### (Dutiyo bhāgo)

### 43. Sakiṃsammajjakavaggo

#### 1. Sakiṃsammajjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassino {pb:T:2.0024}{pb:M:2.0001}{pb:V:2.0001} bhagavato, pāṭaliṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvāva taṃ pādapaggaṃ, tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna, bodhiṃ sammajji tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Sammajjitvāna taṃ bodhiṃ, avandiṃ pāṭaliṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Namassamāno taṃ bodhiṃ, gañchiṃ paṭikuṭiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tādimaggena {pb:V:2.0002} gacchāmi, saranto bodhimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ajagaro maṃ pīḷesi, ghorarūpo mahabbalo.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsanne {pb:P:2.0379} me kataṃ kammaṃ, phalena tosayī mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kaḷevaraṃ me gilati, devaloke ramāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anāvilaṃ mama cittaṃ, visuddhaṃ paṇḍaraṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Sokasallaṃ na jānāmi, cittasantāpanaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca, apamāro vitacchikā;
::

::gathalast
Daddu kaṇḍu ca me natthi, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ {note:sammajjane idaṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soko {pb:M:2.0002} ca paridevo ca, hadaye me na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Abhantaṃ ujukaṃ cittaṃ, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samādhīsu {pb:T:2.0025} na majjāmi {note:samādhīsu na sajjāmi (sī.), samādhiṃ puna pajjāmi (syā)}, visadaṃ hoti mānasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ samādhimicchāmi, so so sampajjate mamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rajanīye na rajjāmi, atho dussaniyesu {note:dosaniyesu (sī. syā. ka.)} ca;
::

::gathalast
Mohanīye na muyhāmi, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito {note:ekanavute ito (sī. syā.)} kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sakiṃsammajjako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sakiṃsammajjakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Ekadussadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:V:2.0003} haṃsavatiyā, ahosiṃ tiṇahārako;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇahārena jīvāmi, tena posemi dārake.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Tamandhakāraṃ nāsetvā, uppajji lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sake {pb:T:2.0026} ghare nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesi tāvade;
::

::gathalast
‘Buddho loke samuppanno, deyyadhammo na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Idaṃ {pb:M:2.0003} me sāṭakaṃ ekaṃ, natthi me koci dāyako;
::

::gathalast
Dukkho nirayasamphasso, ropayissāmi dakkhiṇaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃ dussaṃ gahetvāna, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekaṃ {pb:P:2.0380} dussaṃ daditvāna, ukkuṭṭhiṃ sampavattayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘Yadi buddho tuvaṃ vīra, tārehi maṃ mahāmuni’.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Mama dānaṃ pakittento, akā me anumodanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā ekadussena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappasatasahassāni, vinipātaṃ na gacchasi.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissasi;
::

::gathalast
Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī {note:cakkavatti (syā.)} bhavissasi.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ {note:asaṅkayaṃ (syā. ka.) evamuparipi};
::

::gathalast
Devaloke manusse vā, saṃsaranto tuvaṃ bhave.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Rūpavā guṇasampanno, anavakkantadehavā {note:anuvattanta… (syā)};
::

::gathalast
Akkhobhaṃ amitaṃ dussaṃ, labhissasi yadicchakaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī vīro {note:dhīro (sī. syā.)}, haṃsarājāva ambare.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:2.0027} yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, ekadussassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paduddhāre {pb:V:2.0004} paduddhāre, dussaṃ nibbattate mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Heṭṭhā dussamhi tiṭṭhāmi, uparicchadanaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cakkavāḷaṃ upādāya, sakānanaṃ sapabbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Icchamāno cahaṃ ajja, dussehacchādayeyya taṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Teneva ekadussena, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo hutvāna, saṃsarāmi bhavābhave.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipākaṃ {pb:M:2.0004} viekadussassa, nājjhagaṃ katthacikkhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ayaṃ me antimā jāti, vipaccati idhāpi me.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dussamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekadussassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekadussadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Ekadussadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Ekāsanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:T:2.0028}{pb:P:2.0381}, gosito nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nārado nāma nāmena, kassapo iti maṃ vidū;
::

::gathalast
Suddhimaggaṃ gavesanto, vasāmi gosite tadā.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, agañchi anilañjasā.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanagge gacchamānassa, disvā raṃsiṃ mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Kaṭṭhamañcaṃ paññāpetvā, ajinañca apatthariṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsanaṃ {pb:V:2.0005} paññāpetvāna, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Somanassaṃ paveditvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sallakatto mahāvīra, āturānaṃ tikicchako;
::

::gathalast
Mamaṃ rogaparetassa {note:rāga… (syā.)}, tikicchaṃ dehi nāyaka.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kallatthikā ye passanti, buddhaseṭṭha tuvaṃ mune;
::

::gathalast
Dhuvatthasiddhiṃ papponti, etesaṃ ajaro {note:jajjaro (sī. pī. ka.)} bhave.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na {pb:M:2.0005} me deyyadhammo atthi, pavattaphalabhojihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ me āsanaṃ atthi {note:na me deyyaṃ tava atthi (sī. syā.)}, nisīda kaṭṭhamañcake’.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisīdi tattha bhagavā, asambhītova {note:acchambhitova (syā. ka.)} kesarī;
::

::gathalast
Muhuttaṃ vītināmetvā, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Visaṭṭho {pb:T:2.0029} {note:vissattho (sī. pī), vissaṭṭho (syā. ka.)} hohi mā bhāyi, laddho jotiraso tayā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ tuyhaṃ patthitaṃ sabbaṃ, paripūrissatināgate {note:paripūrissatāsanaṃ (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na moghaṃ taṃ kataṃ tuyhaṃ, puññakkhette anuttare;
::

::gathalast
Sakkā uddharituṃ attā, yassa cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ {note:sunīhitaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Imināsanadānena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Kappasatasahassāni, vinipātaṃ na gacchasi.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissasi;
::

::gathalast
Asītikkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissasi.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ {pb:P:2.0382} vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sukhito hutvā, saṃsāre saṃsarissasi’.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī vīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, sarathaṃ sandamānikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kānanaṃ pavisitvāpi, yadā icchāmi āsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vārimajjhagato santo, yadā icchāmi āsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:2.0006} yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pallaṅkasatasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve {pb:T:2.0030}{pb:M:2.0006} bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Duve kule pajāyāmi, khattiye atha brāhmaṇe.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekāsanaṃ daditvāna, puññakkhette anuttare;
::

::gathalast
Dhammapallaṅkamādāya {note:dhammapallaṅkamaññāya (syā. ka.)}, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekāsanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekāsanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Sattakadambapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre, kukkuṭo {note:kadambo (sī. syā. pī.)} nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Tamhi pabbatapādamhi, satta buddhā vasiṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadambaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satta mālā gahetvāna, puññacittena {note:puṇṇacittena (ka.)} okiriṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:2.0031} kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito {pb:P:2.0383} kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0007} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:2.0007} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattakadambapupphiyo thero imā
::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sattakadambapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 5. Koraṇḍapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanakammiko pure āsiṃ, pitumātumatenahaṃ {note:pitupitāmahenahaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pasumārena jīvāmi, kusalaṃ me na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama āsayasāmantā, tisso lokagganāyako;
::

::gathalast
Padāni tīṇi dassesi, anukampāya cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkante ca pade disvā, tissanāmassa satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, pade cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koraṇḍaṃ {pb:T:2.0032} pupphitaṃ disvā, pādapaṃ dharaṇīruhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakosakaṃ gahetvāna, padaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Koraṇḍavaṇṇakoyeva, suppabhāso bhavāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, padapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koraṇḍapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Koraṇḍapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Ghatamaṇḍadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sucintitaṃ {pb:M:2.0008}{pb:V:2.0008} bhagavantaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upaviṭṭhaṃ mahāraññaṃ, vātābādhena pīḷitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā {pb:T:2.0033} cittaṃ pasādetvā, ghatamaṇḍamupānayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Katattā {pb:P:2.0384} ācitattā ca, gaṅgā bhāgīrathī ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāsamuddā cattāro, ghataṃ sampajjare mama;
::

::gathalast
Ayañca pathavī ghorā, appamāṇā asaṅkhiyā.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, bhavate madhusakkarā;
::

::gathalast
Cātuddīpā {note:catuddisā (syā.)} ime rukkhā, pādapā dharaṇīruhā.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, kapparukkhā bhavanti te;
::

::gathalast
Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ghatamaṇḍassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

::

Abhāsitthāti.

#### 7. Ekadhammassavaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0034} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Catusaccaṃ pakāsento, santāresi bahuṃ janaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:M:2.0009}{pb:V:2.0009} tena samayena, jaṭilo uggatāpano;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhaseṭṭhassa upari, gantuṃ na visahāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Udake vokkamitvāna, evaṃ gacchāmi ambare;
::

::gathalast
Na me idaṃ bhūtapubbaṃ, iriyāpathavikopanaṃ.

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Handa metaṃ gavesissaṃ, appevatthaṃ labheyyahaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;

::gatha1

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

#### 9. Sovaṇṇakiṅkaṇiyattheraapadānaṃ

#### 10. Soṇṇakontarikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nittiṇṇaoghaṃ sambuddhaṃ, jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ muniṃ;

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

167\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
169\.

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.

::centre

::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Soṇṇakontarikattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Sakiṃsammajjakavaggo tecattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sakiṃsammajjako {pb:P:2.0390} thero, ekadussī ekāsanī;
::

::gathalast
Kadambakoraṇḍakado, ghatassavanikopi ca.
::

::gatha1
Sucintiko kiṅkaṇiko, soṇṇakontarikopi ca;
::

::gathalast
Ekagāthāsatañcettha, ekasattatimeva ca.
::

### 44. Ekavihārivaggo

#### 1. Ekavihārikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imamhi {pb:T:2.0044}{pb:M:2.0016}{pb:V:2.0016} bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nippapañco nirālambo, ākāsasamamānaso;
::

::gathalast
Suññatābahulo tādī, animittarato vasī.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asaṅgacitto nikleso {note:nillepo (syā. ka.)}, asaṃsaṭṭho kule gaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Mahākāruṇiko vīro, vinayopāyakovido.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uyyutto parakiccesu, vinayanto sadevake;
::

::gathalast
Nibbānagamanaṃ maggaṃ, gatiṃ paṅkavisosanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amataṃ paramassādaṃ, jarāmaccunivāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahāparisamajjhe so, nisinno lokatārako.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karavīkaruto {note:karavīkarudo (syā. pī. ka.)} nātho, brahmaghoso tathāgato;
::

::gathalast
Uddharanto mahāduggā, vippanaṭṭhe anāyake.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Desento virajaṃ dhammaṃ, diṭṭho me lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbajitvā tadāpāhaṃ, cintento jinasāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekakova vane ramme, vasiṃ saṃsaggapīḷito.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkāyavūpakāso {pb:T:2.0045} me, hetubhūto mamābhavī {note:mamāgamī (syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Manaso vūpakāsassa, saṃsaggabhayadassino.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:P:2.0391} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:2.0017}{pb:V:2.0017} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekavihāriko thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekavihārikattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Ekasaṅkhiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassino bhagavato, mahābodhimaho ahu;
::

::gathalast
Mahājanā samāgamma, pūjenti bodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi taṃ orakaṃ maññe, buddhaseṭṭho bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Yassāyaṃ īdisā bodhi, pūjanīyā {note:īdiso bodhi, pūjanīyo (syā.)} ca satthuno.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato saṅkhaṃ gahetvāna, bodhirukkhamupaṭṭhahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhamanto sabbadivasaṃ, avandiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsannake kataṃ kammaṃ, devalokaṃ apāpayī;
::

::gathalast
Kaḷevaraṃ me patitaṃ, devaloke ramāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni{pb:T:2.0046}, tuṭṭhahaṭṭhā pamoditā;
::

::gathalast
Sadā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhanti, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekasattatime kappe, rājā āsiṃ sudassano;
::

::gathalast
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambumaṇḍassa issaro.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato aṅgasatā turiyā {note:tūrā (sī. ka.)}, parivārenti maṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ, upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mātukucchigatassāpi, vajjare bheriyo sadā.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaṭṭhitvāna sambuddhaṃ, anubhutvāna sampadā;
::

::gathalast
Sivaṃ sukhemaṃ amataṃ, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0018} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:M:2.0018} vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekasaṅkhiyo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekasaṅkhiyattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Pāṭihīrasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0047}{pb:P:2.0392} nāma jino, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Vasīsatasahassehi, nagaraṃ pāvisī tadā.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagaraṃ pavisantassa, upasantassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Ratanāni pajjotiṃsu {note:panādiṃsu (pī.)}, nigghoso āsi tāvade.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhassa ānubhāvena, bherī vajjumaghaṭṭitā;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃ vīṇā pavajjanti, buddhassa pavisato puraṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ namassāmi {note:na passāmi (sī.)}, padumuttaramahāmuniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭihīrañca passitvā, tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthusampadā;
::

::gathalast
Acetanāpi turiyā, sayameva pavajjare.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0048} sudaṃ āyasmā pāṭihīrasaññako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Pāṭihīrasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Ñāṇatthavikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva {pb:M:2.0019}{pb:V:2.0019} jalitaṃ, dīparukkhaṃva jotitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kañcanaṃva virocantaṃ, addasaṃ dvipaduttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kamaṇḍaluṃ ṭhapetvāna, vākacīrañca kuṇḍikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thaviṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ, mohajālasamākulaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇālokaṃ dassetvāna, nittiṇṇosi mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ, sabbāvantamanuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇe te upamā natthi, yāvatājagatogati {note:yāvatā ca gatogati (pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tena ñāṇena sabbaññū, iti buddho pavuccati;
::

::gathalast
Vandāmi taṃ mahāvīraṃ, sabbaññutamanāvaraṃ’.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito {pb:P:2.0393} kappe, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thaviṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ñāṇatthavāyidaṃ phalaṃ;
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo;
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:2.0049} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ñāṇatthaviko thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ñāṇatthavikattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 5. Ucchukhaṇḍikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, dvārapālo ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ucchukhaṇḍikamādāya, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, vipassissa mahesino.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito {pb:M:2.0020}{pb:V:2.0020} kappe, yaṃ ucchumadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ucchukhaṇḍassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
49\.

::gatha1

::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ucchukhaṇḍiko thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ucchukhaṇḍikattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Kaḷambadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Romaso {pb:T:2.0050} nāma sambuddho, vasate pabbatantare;
::

::gathalast
Kaḷambaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kaḷambassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1

54\.

::gatha1

::

Abhāsitthāti.

#### 7. Ambāṭakadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipine {pb:P:2.0394} buddhaṃ disvāna, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ambāṭakaṃ gahetvāna, sayambhussa adāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekatiṃse {pb:V:2.0021} ito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:T:2.0051}{pb:M:2.0021} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
58\.

::hangnum

::

Abhāsitthāti.

::

#### 8. Harītakadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Harītakaṃ āmalakaṃ, ambajambuvibhītakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ billaṃ, sayameva harāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvāna pabbhāragataṃ, jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ muniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ābādhena āpīḷentaṃ, adutīyaṃ mahāmuniṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Harītakaṃ gahetvāna, sayambhussa adāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khādamattamhi bhesajje, byādhi passambhi {note:passaddhi (ka.)} tāvade.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahīnadaratho buddho, anumodamakāsi me;
::

::gathalast
‘Bhesajjadāneniminā, byādhivūpasamena ca.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devabhūto manusso vā, jāto vā aññajātiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sukhito hotu, mā ca te byādhimāgamā’.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:T:2.0052} vatvāna sambuddho, sayambhū aparājito;
::

::gathalast
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī dhīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yato harītakaṃ dinnaṃ, sayambhussa mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ jātiṃ upādāya, byādhi me nupapajjatha.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, bhesajjamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhesajjassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:M:2.0022}{pb:V:2.0022}{pb:P:2.0395} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā harītakadāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Harītakadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 9. Ambapiṇḍiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthirājā tadā āsiṃ, īsādanto uruḷhavā;
::

::gathalast
Vicaranto brahāraññe, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambapiṇḍaṃ {pb:T:2.0053} gahetvāna, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭiggaṇhi mahāvīro, siddhattho lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama nijjhāyamānassa, paribhuñji tadā jino;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ahaṃ cavitvāna, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Eteneva upāyena, anubhutvāna sampadā.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padhānapahitattohaṃ, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambapiṇḍiyo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ambapiṇḍiyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Ambaphaliyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa{pb:T:2.0054}{pb:M:2.0023}{pb:V:2.0023}, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Piṇḍāya vicarantassa, dhārato uttamaṃ yasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggaphalaṃ gahetvāna, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Dakkhiṇeyyassa vīrassa, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena dvipadinda {note:dipadinda (sī. syā. pī.)}, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
::

::gathalast
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito {pb:P:2.0396} kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, aggadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::gathalast
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambaphaliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
::

::centre
Ambaphaliyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Ekavihārivaggo catucattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Thero {pb:T:2.0055} ekavihārī ca, saṅkhiyo pāṭihīrako;
::

::gathalast
Thaviko ucchukhaṇḍī ca, kaḷambaambāṭakado.
::

::gatha1
Harītakambapiṇḍī ca, ambado dasamo yati;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷasīti ca gāthāyo, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
::

### 45. Vibhītakavaggo

#### 1. Vibhītakamiñjiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kakusandho {pb:T:2.0056}{pb:M:2.0024}{pb:V:2.0024} mahāvīro, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Gaṇamhā vūpakaṭṭho so, agamāsi vanantaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bījamiñjaṃ gahetvāna, latāya āvuṇiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhagavā tamhi samaye, jhāyate pabbatantare.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Dakkhiṇeyyassa vīrassa, bījamiñjamadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappamhi, yaṃ miñjamadadiṃ {note:phalamadadiṃ (sī. pī.), bījamadadiṃ (syā.)} tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bījamiñjassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vibhītakamiñjiyo {note:vibhedaka… (syā. ka.)} thero imā
::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Vibhītakamiñjiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Koladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajinena {pb:T:2.0057}{pb:V:2.0025}{pb:P:2.0397} nivatthohaṃ, vākacīradharo tadā;
::

::gathalast
Khāriyā pūrayitvāna, kolaṃhāsiṃ mamassamaṃ {note:khāribhāraṃ haritvāna, kolamāharimassamaṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamhi {pb:M:2.0025} kāle sikhī buddho, eko adutiyo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Mamassamaṃ upāgacchi, jānanto sabbakālikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, vanditvāna ca subbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ubho hatthehi paggayha, kolaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, koladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koladāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Koladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

::

::gathalast

54\.

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Soṇṇapīṭhe akkamāmi {note:soṇṇapīṭhena kamāmi (ka.)}, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

#### 10. Bodhigharadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa {pb:T:2.0065} bhagavato, dvipadindassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, bodhigharamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tusitaṃ upapannomhi, vasāmi ratane ghare;
::

::gathalast
Na me sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā, vāto gatte na samphuse.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcasaṭṭhimhito kappe, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāsikaṃ nāma nagaraṃ, vissakammena {note:visukammena (syā. ka.)} māpitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dasayojanaāyāmaṃ, aṭṭhayojanavitthataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na tamhi nagare atthi, kaṭṭhaṃ vallī ca mattikā.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiriyaṃ yojanaṃ āsi, addhayojanavitthataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṅgalo nāma pāsādo, vissakammena māpito.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni, thambhā soṇṇamayā ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇimayā ca niyyūhā, chadanaṃ rūpiyaṃ ahu.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ {pb:M:2.0031} gharaṃ, vissakammena māpitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhāvutthaṃ mayā etaṃ, gharadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te sabbe anubhotvāna, devamānusake bhave;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhapattomhi nibbānaṃ, santipadamanuttaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, bodhigharamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ {pb:T:2.0066} nābhijānāmi, gharadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0031} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:P:2.0402} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhigharadāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Bodhigharadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Vibhītakavaggo pañcacattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Vibhītakī kolaphalī, billabhallātakappado;
::

::gathalast
Uttalambaṭakī ceva, āsanī pādapīṭhako.
::

::gatha1
Vediko bodhighariko, gāthāyo gaṇitāpi ca;
::

::gathalast
Ekūnāsītikā sabbā, asmiṃ vagge pakittitā.
::

### 46. Jagatidāyakavaggo

#### 1. Jagatidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammadassissa {pb:T:2.0067}{pb:M:2.0032}{pb:V:2.0032} munino, bodhiyā pādaputtame;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, jagatiṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Darito pabbatato vā, rukkhato patito ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cuto patiṭṭhaṃ vindāmi, jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na me corā vihesanti, nātimaññanti khattiyā {note:pasahanti, nātimaññati khattiyo (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbāmittetikkamāmi, jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha pūjito homi, jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, jagatiṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, jagatidānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0068} sudaṃ āyasmā jagatidāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Jagatidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Morahatthiyattheraapadānaṃ

Sumanehi paṭicchannaṃ, dhārayāmi mahāyasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, tālavaṇṭamadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, tālavaṇṭassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumanatālavaṇṭiyo thero imā
::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sumanatālavaṇṭiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Avaṭaphaliyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

#### 9. Sayaṃpaṭibhāniyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kakudhaṃ vilasantaṃva, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamandhakāraṃ nāsetvā, santāretvā bahuṃ janaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇālokena jotantaṃ, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vasīsatasahassehi, nīyantaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uddharantaṃ bahū satte, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āhanantaṃ {note:āhanitvā (syā. ka.)} dhammabheriṃ, maddantaṃ titthiye gaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Sīhanādaṃ vinadantaṃ, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā brahmalokato, āgantvāna sabrahmakā;
::

::gathalast
Pucchanti nipuṇe pañhe, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassañjaliṃ karitvāna, āyācanti sadevakā;
::

::gathalast
Tena puññaṃ anubhonti, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe {pb:V:2.0044} janā samāgantvā, sampavārenti cakkhumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na vikampati ajjhiṭṭho, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagaraṃ {pb:T:2.0084} pavisato yassa, ravanti bheriyo bahū;
::

::gathalast
Vinadanti gajā mattā, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīthiyā {note:rathiyā (sī.)} gacchato yassa, sabbābhā jotate sadā;
::

::gathalast
Abbhunnatā samā honti, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Byāharantassa {pb:P:2.0411} buddhassa, cakkavāḷampi suyyati;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe satte viññāpeti, ko disvā na pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito {pb:M:2.0044} kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhikittayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum

Abhāsitthāti.

#### 10. Nimittabyākaraṇiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā himavaṃ, mante vāce mahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Catupaññāsasahassāni, sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhitā {pb:T:2.0085} vedagū sabbe, chaḷaṅge pāramiṃ gatā;
::

::gathalast
Sakavijjāhupatthaddhā, himavante vasanti te.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cavitvā tusitā kāyā, devaputto mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Uppajji mātukucchismiṃ, sampajāno patissato.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambuddhe upapajjante, dasasahassi kampatha;
::

::gathalast
Andhā cakkhuṃ alabhiṃsu, uppajjantamhi nāyake.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbākāraṃ {pb:V:2.0045} pakampittha, kevalā vasudhā ayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nigghosasaddaṃ sutvāna, ubbijjiṃsu {note:vimhayiṃsu (syā. ka.)} mahājanā.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe janā samāgamma, āgacchuṃ mama santikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vasudhāyaṃ pakampittha, kiṃ vipāko bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avacāsiṃ {note:vidassāmi (syā.)} tadā tesaṃ, mā bhetha {note:mā roda (ka.), mābhāyittha (syā.)} natthi vo bhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Visaṭṭhā hotha sabbepi, uppādoyaṃ suvatthiko {note:sukhatthiko (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhahetūhi {pb:M:2.0045} samphussa {note:aṭṭhahetūhi samphassa (syā. pī.), atthahetu nisaṃsayaṃ (ka.)}, vasudhāyaṃ pakampati;
::

::gathalast
Tathā nimittā dissanti, obhāso vipulo mahā.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho, uppajjissati cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Saññāpetvāna janataṃ, pañcasīle kathesahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvāna {pb:P:2.0412} pañca sīlāni, buddhuppādañca dullabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ubbegajātā sumanā, tuṭṭhahaṭṭhā ahaṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ nimittaṃ viyākariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, byākaraṇassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:T:2.0086} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nimittabyākaraṇiyo thero imā
::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Nimittabyākaraṇiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Sālakusumiyavaggo sattacattālīsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sālakusumiyo thero, pūjā nibbāpakopi ca;
::

::gathalast
Setudo tālavaṇṭī ca, avaṭalabujappado.
::

::gatha1
Pilakkhapaṭibhānī ca, veyyākaraṇiyo dijo;
::

::gathalast
Dvesattati ca gāthāyo, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
::

### 48. Naḷamālivaggo

#### 1. Naḷamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ {pb:T:2.0087}{pb:M:2.0046}{pb:V:2.0046} sambuddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vipinaggena gacchantaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naḷamālaṃ gahetvāna, nikkhamanto ca tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, naḷamālamapūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dakkhiṇeyyaṃ mahāvīraṃ, sabbalokānukampakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ mālamabhiropayiṃ {note:pupphamabhiropayiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷamāliyo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Naḷamāliyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Maṇipūjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0088}{pb:V:2.0047}{pb:P:2.0413} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, gacchate anilañjase.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avidūre himavantassa, mahājātassaro ahu;
::

::gathalast
Tattha me bhavanaṃ āsi, puññakammena saṃyutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavanā {pb:M:2.0047} abhinikkhamma, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Indīvaraṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vicinaṃ naddasaṃ pupphaṃ, pūjayissanti nāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, avandiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama sīse maṇiṃ gayha, pūjayiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imāya maṇipūjāya, vipāko hotu bhaddako.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘So te ijjhatu saṅkappo, labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imāya maṇipūjāya, anubhohi mahāyasaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna bhagavā, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Agamāsi buddhaseṭṭho, yattha cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhikappāni devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anekasatakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbakammaṃ {pb:T:2.0089} sarantassa, devabhūtassa me sato;
::

::gathalast
Maṇi nibbattate mayhaṃ, ālokakaraṇo mamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chaḷasītisahassāni, nāriyo me pariggahā;
::

::gathalast
Vicittavatthābharaṇā, āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā {note:āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aḷārapamhā hasulā, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
::

::gathalast
Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ, maṇipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soṇṇamayā maṇimayā, lohitaṅgamayā tathā;
::

::gathalast
Bhaṇḍā me sukatā honti, yadicchasi {note:yadicchāya (sī. pī.)} piḷandhanā.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kūṭāgārā {pb:V:2.0048} gahārammā, sayanañca mahārahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābhā tesaṃ suladdhañca, ye labhanti upassutiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puññakkhettaṃ manussānaṃ, osadhaṃ sabbapāṇinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayhampi {pb:M:2.0048}{pb:P:2.0414} sukataṃ kammaṃ, yohaṃ adakkhi nāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vinipātā pamuttomhi, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Divasañceva rattiñca {note:samantā sattaratanā (sī. pī. ka.)}, āloko hoti me sadā.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāyeva maṇipūjāya, anubhotvāna sampadā;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇāloko mayā diṭṭho, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ maṇiṃ abhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, maṇipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:T:2.0090} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maṇipūjako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Maṇipūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Ukkāsatikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kosiko nāma bhagavā, cittakūṭe vasī tadā;
::

::gathalast
Jhāyī jhānarato buddho, vivekābhirato muni.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā {note:ajjhogahetvā (sī. syā. pī.)} himavantaṃ, nārīgaṇapurakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ kosikaṃ buddhaṃ, puṇṇamāyeva candimaṃ.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ukkāsate gahetvāna, parivāresahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Sattarattindivaṃ ṭhatvā {note:buddho (syā. ka.)}, aṭṭhamena agacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vuṭṭhitaṃ {pb:V:2.0049} kosikaṃ buddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto vanditvā, ekaṃ bhikkhaṃ adāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjiṃ tusite kāye, ekabhikkhāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Divasañceva {pb:T:2.0091}{pb:M:2.0049} rattiñca, āloko hoti me sadā;
::

::gathalast
Samantā yojanasataṃ, obhāsena pharāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcapaññāsakappamhi, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambumaṇḍassa {note:jambusaṇḍassa (pī.)} issaro.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā me nagaraṃ āsi, iddhaṃ phītaṃ sunimmitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tiṃsayojanamāyāmaṃ, vitthārena ca vīsati.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sobhaṇaṃ nāma nagaraṃ, vissakammena māpitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dasasaddāvivittaṃ taṃ, sammatāḷasamāhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:P:2.0415} tamhi nagare atthi, vallikaṭṭhañca mattikā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃyeva, jotate niccakālikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catupākāraparikkhittaṃ, tayo āsuṃ maṇimayā;
::

::gathalast
Vemajjhe tālapantī ca, vissakammena māpitā.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dasasahassapokkharañño, padumuppalachāditā;
::

::gathalast
Puṇḍarīkehi {note:puṇḍarīkādi (syā.)} sañchannā, nānāgandhasamīritā.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ ukkaṃ dhārayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ukkadhārassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:2.0092} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ukkāsatiko thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ukkāsatikattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

77\.

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Naḷamālī maṇidado, ukkāsatikabījanī;

::gathalast

Vallikāro {pb:T:2.0099} pānadhido, atho pulinacaṅkamo;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāyo pañcanavuti, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.

### 49. Paṃsukūlavaggo

#### 1. Paṃsukūlasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tisso {pb:M:2.0055}{pb:V:2.0055} nāmāsi bhagavā, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Paṃsukūlaṃ ṭhapetvāna, vihāraṃ pāvisī jino.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vinataṃ {note:sajjitaṃ (syā.), tiyantaṃ (pī.)} dhanumādāya, bhakkhatthāya cariṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇḍalaggaṃ gahetvāna, kānanaṃ pāvisiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasaṃ {pb:P:2.0419} paṃsukūlaṃ, dumagge laggitaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Cāpaṃ tattheva nikkhippa, sire katvāna añjaliṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, vipulāya ca pītiyā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, paṃsukūlaṃ avandahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, paṃsukūlamavandahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:T:2.0100} vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paṃsukūlasaññako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Paṃsukūlasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Buddhasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhāyako {pb:V:2.0056} mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca, sanighaṇḍusakeṭubhe.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nadīsotapaṭibhāgā{pb:M:2.0056}, sissā āyanti me tadā;
::

::gathalast
Tesāhaṃ mante {note:mantaṃ (syā. ka.)} vācemi, rattindivamatandito.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhattho nāma sambuddho, loke uppajji tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Tamandhakāraṃ nāsetvā, ñāṇālokaṃ pavattayi.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama aññataro sisso, sissānaṃ so kathesi me;
::

::gathalast
Sutvāna te etamatthaṃ, ārocesuṃ mamaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Tassānuvattati jano, lābho amhaṃ na vijjati {note:na hessati (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhiccuppattikā buddhā, cakkhumanto mahāyasā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃnūnāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ, passeyyaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajinaṃ {pb:T:2.0101} me gahetvāna, vākacīraṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ;
::

::gathalast
Assamā abhinikkhamma, sisse āmantayiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Odumbarikapupphaṃva, candamhi sasakaṃ yathā;
::

::gathalast
Vāyasānaṃ yathā khīraṃ, dullabho lokanāyako {note:dullabhā lokanāyakā (sī.), dullabhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho lokamhi uppanno, manussattampi dullabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ubhosu vijjamānesu, savanañca sudullabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, cakkhuṃ lacchāma no bhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etha sabbe gamissāma, sammāsambuddhasantikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kamaṇḍaludharā {pb:P:2.0420} sabbe, kharājinanivāsino;
::

::gathalast
Te jaṭā bhārabharitā, nikkhamuṃ vipinā tadā.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yugamattaṃ pekkhamānā, uttamatthaṃ gavesino;
::

::gathalast
Āsattidosarahitā, asambhītāva kesarī.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appakiccā aloluppā, nipakā santavuttino;
::

::gathalast
Uñchāya caramānā te, buddhaseṭṭhamupāgamuṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Diyaḍḍhayojane {pb:V:2.0057} sese, byādhi me upapajjatha;
::

::gathalast
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito {pb:M:2.0057} kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:T:2.0102} vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Buddhasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Bhisadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ogayha yaṃ {note:ogayhāhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} pokkharaṇiṃ, nānākuñjarasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uddharāmi bhisaṃ tattha, ghāsahetu {note:asanahetu (syā.)} ahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, padumuttarasavhayo;
::

::gathalast
Rattambaradharo {note:rattakambaladharo (syā.)} buddho, gacchati anilañjase.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhunanto paṃsukūlāni, saddamassosahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Uddhaṃ nijjhāyamānohaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattheva ṭhitako santo, āyāciṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Madhuṃ bhisehi savati, khīraṃ sappiṃ muḷālibhi.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggaṇhātu me buddho, anukampāya cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Tato kāruṇiko satthā, oruhitvā mahāyaso.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggaṇhi mamaṃ bhikkhaṃ, anukampāya cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho, akā me anumodanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sukhī {pb:T:2.0103} hotu {note:hohi (sī. syā. pī. ka.)} mahāpuñña, gati tuyhaṃ samijjhatu;
::

::gathalast
Iminā bhisadānena, labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:V:2.0058}{pb:P:2.0421} vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhamādāya sambuddho, ambarenāgamā jino.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:2.0058} bhisaṃ gahetvāna, āgacchiṃ mama assamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhisaṃ rukkhe lagetvāna {note:laggitvāna (syā. ka.)}, mama dānamanussariṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāvāto vuṭṭhahitvā, sañcālesi vanaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato me asanipāto, matthake nipatī tadā;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ nisinnako santo, tattha kālaṅkato ahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puññakammena saṃyutto, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kaḷevaraṃ me patitaṃ, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chaḷasītisahassāni, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ bhisaṃ {note:bhikkhaṃ (sabbattha)} adadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast

#### 4. Ñāṇathavikattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
46\.

::gatha1
‘‘Dakkhiṇe {pb:V:2.0059} himavantassa, sukato assamo mama;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābhālābhena {pb:M:2.0059} santuṭṭho, mūlena ca phalena ca;
::

::gathalast
Anvesanto ācariyaṃ, vasāmi ekako ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, loke uppajji tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Catusaccaṃ pakāseti, uddharanto mahājanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ suṇomi sambuddhaṃ, napi me koci saṃsati {note:bhāsati (sī.), sāsati (syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhavasse atikkante, assosiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.

::gatha1
‘‘Aggidāruṃ {pb:P:2.0422} nīharitvā, sammajjitvāna assamaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
51\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, sumedho lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Uddharanto bahū satte, deseti amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Janakāyamatikkamma, vanditvā jinasāgaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca, dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parāyano {note:parāyaṇo (sī. pī.)} patiṭṭhā ca, dīpo ca dvipaduttamo.
::

::centre
Ekavīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nepuñño dassane vīro, tāresi janataṃ tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sakkā theve {note:have (sī. pī.) bhave (syā. ka.)} kusaggena, pametuṃ sāgaruttame {note:sāgaruttamo (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Natveva tava sabbaññu, ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave.
::

::hangnum
57\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
58\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
60\.

::gatha1
‘‘Chahi {pb:T:2.0106} gāthāhi sabbaññuṃ, kittayitvā mahāyasaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
62\.

::gatha1

65\.

67\.

::

::gathalast

#### 5. Candanamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, piyarūpe manorame;
::

::gathalast
Asītikoṭiyo hitvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbajitvāna kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, nadīkūle vasāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekakaṃ {pb:T:2.0108} maṃ viharantaṃ, buddhaseṭṭho upāgami;
::

::gathalast
Nāhaṃ jānāmi buddhoti, akāsiṃ paṭisantharaṃ {note:paṭisandhāraṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karitvā paṭisanthāraṃ, nāmagottamapucchahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘Devatānusi gandhabbo, adu sakko purindado.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, mahābrahmā idhāgato;
::

::gathalast
Virocesi disā sabbā, udayaṃ sūriyo yathā.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sahassārāni {pb:P:2.0424} cakkāni, pāde dissanti mārisa;
::

::gatha2
Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāmagottaṃ pavedehi, saṃsayaṃ apanehi me’.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Namhi devo na gandhabbo, namhi {note:nāpi (sī.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Brahmabhāvo ca me natthi, etesaṃ uttamo ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Atīto visayaṃ tesaṃ, dālayiṃ kāmabandhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe kilese jhāpetvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:M:2.0062}{pb:V:2.0062} vācaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
85\.

86\.

#### 7. Pulinuppādakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbate {pb:V:2.0064}{pb:P:2.0426} himavantamhi, devalo nāma tāpaso;
::

::gathalast
Tattha me caṅkamo āsi, amanussehi māpito.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jaṭābhārena {pb:T:2.0112} {note:jaṭābhārassa (syā. ka.)} bharito, kamaṇḍaludharo sadā;

::gathalast

::gatha1

116\.

::gathalast

#### 8. Taraṇiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
148\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Udakā abhinikkhamma, kacchapo vārigocaro;

::hangnum
150\.

#### 9. Dhammaruciyattheraapadānaṃ

165\.

166\.

185\.
::

#### 10. Sālamaṇḍapiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
190\.

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā {pb:V:2.0070} sālavanaṃ, sukato assamo mama;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyadassī ca bhagavā, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assamā abhinikkhamma, pavanaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mūlaphalaṃ gavesanto, āhiṇḍāmi vane tadā.
::

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ {pb:T:2.0121} sambuddhaṃ, piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sunisinnaṃ samāpannaṃ, virocantaṃ mahāvane.
::

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catudaṇḍe {pb:M:2.0071} ṭhapetvāna, buddhassa uparī ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā, sālapupphehi chādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattāhaṃ dhārayitvāna, maṇḍapaṃ sālachāditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, buddhaseṭṭhamavandahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
196\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā {pb:P:2.0432} tamhi samaye, vuṭṭhahitvā samādhito;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
197\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvako varuṇo nāma, piyadassissa satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Vasīsatasahassehi, upagacchi vināyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
198\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyadassī ca bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, sitaṃ pātukarī jino.
::

::hangnum
199\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anuruddho upaṭṭhāko, piyadassissa satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā, apucchittha mahāmuniṃ.
::

::hangnum
200\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ko nu kho bhagavā hetu, sitakammassa satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Kāraṇe vijjamānamhi, satthā pātukare sitaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
201\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sattāhaṃ sālacchadanaṃ {note:pupphachadanaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, yo me dhāresi māṇavo;
::

::gathalast
Tassa kammaṃ saritvāna, sitaṃ pātukariṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
202\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Anokāsaṃ na passāmi, yattha {note:yaṃ taṃ (syā. pī. ka.)} puññaṃ vipaccati;
::

::gathalast
Devaloke {pb:T:2.0122} manusse vā, okāsova na sammati.
::

::hangnum
203\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devaloke {pb:V:2.0071} vasantassa, puññakammasamaṅgino;
::

::gathalast
Yāvatā parisā tassa, sālacchannā bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
204\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tattha dibbehi naccehi, gītehi vāditehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Ramissati sadā santo, puññakammasamāhito.
::

::hangnum
205\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yāvatā parisā tassa, gandhagandhī bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Sālassa pupphavasso ca, pavassissati tāvade.
::

::hangnum
206\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tato cutoyaṃ manujo, mānusaṃ āgamissati;
::

::gathalast
Idhāpi sālacchadanaṃ, sabbakālaṃ dharissati {note:dhariyati (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
207\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Idha {pb:M:2.0072} naccañca gītañca, sammatāḷasamāhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
208\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Uggacchante ca sūriye, sālavassaṃ pavassati;
::

::gathalast
Puññakammena saṃyuttaṃ, vassate sabbakālikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
209\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
210\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
::

::hangnum
211\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dhammaṃ abhisamentassa, sālacchannaṃ bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Citake jhāyamānassa, chadanaṃ tattha hessati’.
::

::hangnum
212\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipākaṃ kittayitvāna, piyadassī mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Parisāya dhammaṃ desesi, tappento dhammavuṭṭhiyā.
::

::hangnum
213\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappāni {pb:T:2.0123}{pb:P:2.0433} devesu, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhi ca sattakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
214\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokā idhāgantvā, labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idhāpi sālacchadanaṃ, maṇḍapassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
215\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
::

::gathalast
Idhāpi sālacchadanaṃ, hessati sabbakālikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
216\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāmuniṃ tosayitvā, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
217\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhārase {pb:V:2.0072} kappasate, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
218\.
::

::gatha1
Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
219\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
220\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ {pb:M:2.0073} sudaṃ āyasmā sālamaṇḍapiyo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sālamaṇḍapiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Paṃsukūlavaggo ekūnapaññāsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Paṃsukūlaṃ {pb:T:2.0124} buddhasaññī, bhisado ñāṇakittako;
::

::gathalast
Candanī dhātupūjī ca, pulinuppādakopi ca.
::

::gatha1
Taraṇo dhammaruciko, sālamaṇḍapiyo tathā;
::

::gathalast
Satāni dve honti gāthā, ūnavīsatimeva ca.
::

### 50. Kiṅkaṇipupphavaggo

#### 1. Tikiṅkaṇipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva {pb:T:2.0125}{pb:M:2.0074}{pb:V:2.0073} jotantaṃ, nisinnaṃ pabbatantare;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tīṇi kiṅkaṇipupphāni, paggayha abhiropayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhamabhipūjetvā, gacchāmi dakkhiṇāmukho.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:P:2.0434} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tikiṅkaṇipupphiyo thero imā
::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Tikiṅkaṇipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 8. Pulinathūpiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:M:2.0079}, yamako nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nārado nāma nāmena, jaṭilo uggatāpano;
::

::gathalast
Catuddasasahassāni, sissā paricaranti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisallīnako santo, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
‘Sabbo jano maṃ pūjeti, nāhaṃ pūjemi kiñcanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na me ovādako atthi, vattā koci na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Anācariyupajjhāyo, vane vāsaṃ upemahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Upāsamāno yamahaṃ, garucittaṃ upaṭṭhahe;
::

::gathalast
So me ācariyo natthi, vanavāso niratthako.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Āyāgaṃ me gavesissaṃ, garuṃ bhāvaniyaṃ tathā;
::

::gathalast
Sāvassayo vasissāmi, na koci garahissati’.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uttānakūlā nadikā, supatitthā manoramā;
::

::gathalast
Saṃsuddhapulinākiṇṇā, avidūre mamassamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nadiṃ {pb:T:2.0133} amarikaṃ nāma, upagantvānahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Saṃvaḍḍhayitvā pulinaṃ, akaṃ pulinacetiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:P:2.0438} te ahesuṃ sambuddhā, bhavantakaraṇā munī;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ etādiso thūpo, taṃ nimittaṃ karomahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karitvā {pb:V:2.0079} pulinaṃ {note:puḷine (sī. syā. pī.)} thūpaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphāni, sahasse tīṇi pūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāyapātaṃ namassāmi, vedajāto katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, vandiṃ pulinacetiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā kilesā jāyanti, vitakkā gehanissitā;
::

::gathalast
Sarāmi sukataṃ thūpaṃ, paccavekkhāmi tāvade.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upanissāya viharaṃ, satthavāhaṃ vināyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kilese saṃvaseyyāsi, na yuttaṃ tava mārisa.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saha {pb:M:2.0080} āvajjite thūpe, gāravaṃ hoti me tadā;
::

::gathalast
Kuvitakke vinodesiṃ, nāgo tuttaṭṭito yathā.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ viharamānaṃ maṃ, maccurājābhimaddatha;
::

::gathalast
Tattha kālaṅkato santo, brahmalokamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatāyuṃ vasitvāna, tidive {note:tidase (sī. pī.)} upapajjahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asītikkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphānaṃ {pb:T:2.0134} {note:tesaṃ kiṅkaṇipupphānaṃ (sī.)}, vipākaṃ anubhomahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhātīsatasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ {note:me (ka.)} bhave.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Thūpassa pariciṇṇattā, rajojallaṃ na limpati;
::

::gathalast
Gatte sedā na muccanti, suppabhāso bhavāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aho me sukato thūpo, sudiṭṭhāmarikā nadī;
::

::gathalast
Thūpaṃ katvāna pulinaṃ, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalaṃ kattukāmena, jantunā sāragāhinā;
::

::gathalast
Natthi khettaṃ akhettaṃ vā, paṭipattīva sādhakā {note:sārikā (pī.), sārakā (syā.), sāratā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi balavā poso, aṇṇavaṃ taritussahe;
::

::gathalast
Parittaṃ kaṭṭhamādāya, pakkhandeyya mahāsaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imāhaṃ kaṭṭhaṃ nissāya, tarissāmi mahodadhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ussāhena vīriyena, tareyya udadhiṃ naro.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatheva {pb:V:2.0080}{pb:P:2.0439} me kataṃ kammaṃ, parittaṃ thokakañca yaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ kammaṃ upanissāya, saṃsāraṃ samatikkamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto, mahāsāle suaḍḍhake.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā mātā pitā mayhaṃ, buddhassa saraṇaṃ gatā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bodhipapaṭikaṃ {pb:M:2.0081} gayha, soṇṇathūpamakārayuṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uposathamhi {pb:T:2.0135} divase, soṇṇathūpaṃ vinīharuṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saha disvānahaṃ {note:pasādetvānahaṃ (ka.)} thūpaṃ, sariṃ pulinacetiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekāsane nisīditvā, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::centre
Dvāvīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gavesamāno taṃ vīraṃ, dhammasenāpatiddasaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
87\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
89\.

::

::gathalast

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.

::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::centre

::centre

#### 9. Naḷakuṭidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

95\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::hangnum

::gatha1

#### 10. Piyālaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Migaluddo {pb:V:2.0082} pure āsiṃ, vipine vicaraṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyālaphalamādāya, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puññakkhettassa vīrassa, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekatiṃse {pb:M:2.0083} ito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:P:2.0441} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:2.0138} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piyālaphaladāyako thero imā
::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Piyālaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kiṅkaṇipupphavaggo paññāsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kiṅkaṇī paṃsukūlañca, koraṇḍamatha kiṃsukaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upaḍḍhadussī ghatado, udakaṃ thūpakārako.
::

::gatha1
Naḷakārī ca navamo, piyālaphaladāyako;
::

::gathalast
Satamekañca gāthānaṃ, navakañca taduttari.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Metteyyavaggo bhaddāli, sakiṃsammajjakopi ca;
::

::gathalast
Ekavihārī vibhītakī, jagatī sālapupphiyo.
::

::gatha1
Naḷāgāraṃ paṃsukūlaṃ, kiṅkaṇipupphiyo tathā;
::

::gathalast
Asīti dve ca gāthāyo, catuddasasatāni ca.
::

::centre
Metteyyavaggadasakaṃ.
::

::centre
Pañcamasatakaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 51. Kaṇikāravaggo

#### 1. Tikaṇikārapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho {pb:T:2.0139}{pb:M:2.0084}{pb:V:2.0083} nāma sambuddho, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, himavantamupāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhogayha himavantaṃ, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
::

::gathalast
Pallaṅkamābhujitvāna, nisīdi purisuttamo.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vijjādharo tadā āsiṃ, antalikkhacaro ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tisūlaṃ sukataṃ gayha, gacchāmi ambare tadā.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbatagge yathā aggi, puṇṇamāyeva candimā;
::

::gathalast
Vane obhāsate buddho, sālarājāva phullito.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanaggā {pb:P:2.0442} nikkhamitvāna, buddharaṃsībhidhāvare;
::

::gathalast
Naḷaggivaṇṇasaṅkāsā, disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vicinaṃ addasaṃ pupphaṃ, kaṇikāraṃ devagandhikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tīṇi pupphāni ādāya, buddhaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhassa ānubhāvena, tīṇi pupphāni me tadā;
::

::gathalast
Uddhaṃvaṇṭā adhopattā, chāyaṃ kubbanti satthuno.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha {pb:T:2.0140} me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, kaṇikārīti ñāyati;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassakaṇḍaṃ satabheṇḍu {note:satageṇḍu (syā.)}, dhajāluharitāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satasahassaniyyūhā, byamhe pātubhaviṃsu me.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soṇṇamayā maṇimayā, lohitaṅgamayāpi ca;
::

::gathalast
Phalikāpi ca pallaṅkā, yenicchakā yadicchakā {note:yenicchayā yadicchakaṃ (syā.), yadicchakāyadicchakā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahārahañca {pb:M:2.0085}{pb:V:2.0084} sayanaṃ, tūlikāvikatīyutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uddhalomikaekantaṃ, bimbohanasamāyutaṃ {note:bibbohanasamāyutaṃ… (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavanā nikkhamitvāna, caranto devacārikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yadā icchāmi gamanaṃ, devasaṅghapurakkhato.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphassa heṭṭhā tiṭṭhāmi, uparicchadanaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Samantā yojanasataṃ, kaṇikārehi chāditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni, sāyapātamupaṭṭhahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ, rattindivamatanditā.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha naccehi gītehi, tāḷehi vāditehi ca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, modāmi tidase tadā;
::

::gathalast
Nārīgaṇehi sahito, modāmi byamhamuttame.

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1

19\.

::gathalast

20\.

::hangnum
27\.

::

::gatha2

::gathalast
Ñātīnaṃ uttamo homi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi{pb:P:2.0444}, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:2.0143}{pb:M:2.0087}{pb:V:2.0086} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tikaṇikārapupphiyo thero imā
::

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Tikaṇikārapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Ekapattadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, kumbhakāro ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukataṃ mattikāpattaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pattaṃ datvā bhagavato, ujubhūtassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhave nibbattamānohaṃ, soṇṇathāle labhāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rūpimaye ca sovaṇṇe, taṭṭike ca maṇīmaye.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pātiyo paribhuñjāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yasānañca dhanānañca {note:yasasāva janānañca (syā.)}, aggabhūto {note:pattabhūto (sī. pī.)} ca homahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi bhaddake khette, bījaṃ appampi ropitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sammādhāraṃ pavacchante, phalaṃ toseti kassakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathevidaṃ pattadānaṃ, buddhakhettamhi ropitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pītidhāre pavassante, phalaṃ maṃ tosayissati.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā khettā vijjanti, saṅghāpi ca gaṇāpi ca;
::

::gathalast
Buddhakhettasamo natthi, sukhado sabbapāṇinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namo {pb:T:2.0144} te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
::

::gathalast
Ekapattaṃ daditvāna, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pattamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0087} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:M:2.0088} vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapattadāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre

‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ketakapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ketakapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 9. Sabbaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Varuṇo {pb:T:2.0159}{pb:V:2.0097}{pb:P:2.0452} nāma nāmena, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Chaḍḍetvā dasaputtāni, vanamajjhogahiṃ tadā.

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assamaṃ {pb:M:2.0098} sukataṃ katvā, suvibhattaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi mama assamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi, obhāso vipulo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, pajjalī vipinaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvāna taṃ pāṭihīraṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ, sahakhārimadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anukampāya me buddho, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna, pacchato ehi me tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paribhutte ca saṅghamhi, puññaṃ tava bhavissati’.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puṭakantaṃ gahetvāna, bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha dibbehi naccehi, gītehi vāditehi ca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
60\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:2.0160} yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā caturo dīpā, sasamuddā sapabbatā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā me pakkhigaṇā, ākāse uppatanti ce;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
64\.

::

::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

69\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::gathalast

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
74\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kurañciyaṃ kapitthañca, kosambamatha ketakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāgapupphajjunañceva, kuṭajī ghosasaññako.
::

::gatha1
Thero {pb:T:2.0163} ca sabbaphalado, tathā padumadhāriko;
::

::gathalast
Asīti cettha gāthāyo, tisso gāthā taduttari.
::

### 53. Tiṇadāyakavaggo

#### 1. Tiṇamuṭṭhidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre{pb:M:2.0101}{pb:V:2.0100}, lambako nāma pabbato;
::

::gathalast
Tattheva tisso {note:tatthopatisso (sī. pī. ka.)} sambuddho, abbhokāsamhi caṅkami.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Migaluddo pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvāna taṃ devadevaṃ, tiṇamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisīdanatthaṃ buddhassa, datvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, pakkāmiṃ {note:pakkamiṃ (ka.)} uttarāmukho.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aciraṃ gatamattassa {note:gatamattaṃ maṃ (sī. syā.)}, migarājā apothayi {note:aheṭhayi (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sīhena pothito {note:pātito (sī. pī.), ghāṭito (syā.)} santo, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsanne me kataṃ kammaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhe anāsave;
::

::gathalast
Sumutto saravegova, devalokamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yūpo tattha subho āsi, puññakammābhinimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sahassakaṇḍo satabheṇḍu, dhajālu haritāmayo.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhā {pb:T:2.0164} niddhāvate tassa, sataraṃsīva uggato;
::

::gathalast
Ākiṇṇo devakaññāhi, āmodiṃ kāmakāmihaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokā {pb:P:2.0455} cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Āgantvāna manussattaṃ, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, nisīdanamadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, tiṇamuṭṭhe idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:2.0102}{pb:V:2.0101} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇamuṭṭhidāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Tiṇamuṭṭhidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Mañcadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

14\.

::gatha1

#### 3. Saraṇagamaniyattheraapadānaṃ

::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Saraṇagamaniyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Abbhañjanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:P:2.0456} bandhumatiyā, rājuyyāne vasāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cammavāsī tadā āsiṃ, kamaṇḍaludharo ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addasaṃ vimalaṃ buddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbakāmasamiddhiñca, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvā pasanno sumano, abbhañjanamadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, abbhañjanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0167} sudaṃ āyasmā abbhañjanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Abbhañjanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 8. Bodhisammajjakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ pure bodhipattaṃ, ujjhitaṃ cetiyaṅgaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ gahetvāna chaḍḍesiṃ, alabhiṃ vīsatīguṇe.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa kammassa tejena, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
::

::gathalast
Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte cāpi mānuse.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, āgantvā mānusaṃ bhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṅgapaccaṅgasampanno, ārohapariṇāhavā;
::

::gathalast
Abhirūpo suci homi, sampuṇṇaṅgo anūnako.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devaloke {pb:T:2.0170}{pb:V:2.0105} manusse vā, jāto vā yattha katthaci;
::

::gathalast
