::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mudukā {pb:M:2.0106}{pb:P:2.0458} maddavā sniddhā {note:mudu maddavā siniddhā (syā.)}, sukhumā sukumārikā;
::

::gathalast
Chavi me sabbadā hoti, bodhipatte suchaḍḍite {note:suchaḍḍine (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yato kutoci gatīsu, sarīre samudāgate;
::

::gathalast
Na limpati rajojallaṃ, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṇhe vātātape tassa, aggitāpena vā pana;
::

::gathalast
Gatte sedā na muccanti, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca, tilakā piḷakā tathā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

::

::gathalast

63\.

#### 10. Sugandhattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anubyañjanasampanno, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assāsetā yathā cando, sūriyova pabhaṅkaro;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dharaṇīriva {pb:P:2.0460} sīlena, himavāva samādhinā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa kadāci mahāvīro, parisāsu visārado;
::

::gathalast
Saccāni sampakāseti, uddharanto mahājanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā hi bārāṇasiyaṃ, seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Āsahaṃ dhanadhaññassa {note:anantadhanadhaññassa (ka.)}, pahūtassa bahū tadā.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ, migadāyamupeccahaṃ {note:mupesahaṃ (ka.)};

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Visaṭṭhakantavacanaṃ{pb:T:2.0174}, karavīkasamassaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Haṃsarutehi {note:haṃsadundubhi (syā. pī.)} nigghosaṃ, viññāpentaṃ mahājanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā {pb:M:2.0109} devātidevaṃ taṃ, sutvāva madhuraṃ giraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahāyanappake bhoge, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:V:2.0108} pabbajito cāhaṃ, na cirena bahussuto;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāparisamajjhehaṃ, haṭṭhacitto punappunaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇayiṃ hemavaṇṇassa, vaṇṇaṃ vaṇṇavisārado.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa khīṇāsavo buddho, anīgho chinnasaṃsayo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakammakkhayaṃ patto, vimuttopadhisaṅkhaye.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa so bhagavā buddho, esa sīho anuttaro;
::

::gathalast
Sadevakassa lokassa, brahmacakkappavattako.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Danto dametā santo ca, sametā nibbuto isi;
::

::gathalast
Nibbāpetā ca assattho, assāsetā mahājanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīro sūro ca vikkanto {note:dhīro ca (sī. pī.)}, pañño kāruṇiko vasī;
::

::gathalast
Vijitāvī ca sa jino, appagabbo anālayo.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aneñjo acalo dhīmā, amoho asamo muni;
::

::gathalast
Dhorayho usabho nāgo, sīho sakko garūsupi.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Virāgo vimalo brahmā, vādī sūro raṇañjaho;
::

::gathalast
Akhilo ca visallo ca, asamo saṃyato {note:vusabho (syā.), payato (pī.)} suci.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brāhmaṇo {pb:T:2.0175}{pb:P:2.0461} samaṇo nātho, bhisakko sallakattako;
::

::gathalast
Yodho buddho sutāsuto {note:suto suto (sī. pī.)}, acalo mudito sito {note:dito (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhātā dhatā ca santi ca, kattā netā pakāsitā;
::

::gathalast
Sampahaṃsitā bhettā ca, chettā sotā pasaṃsitā.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akhilo ca visallo ca, anīgho akathaṃkathī;
::

::gathalast
Anejo virajo kattā, gandhā vattā pasaṃsitā.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāretā atthakāretā, kāretā sampadāritā;
::

::gathalast
Pāpetā sahitā kantā, hantā ātāpī tāpaso {note:hantā, tāpitā ca visositā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samacitto {pb:M:2.0110} {note:saccaṭṭhito (syā.)} samasamo, asahāyo dayālayo {note:dayāsayo (sī.)};
::

Accherasatto {note:accheramanto (syā.)} akuho, katāvī isisattamo.

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nittiṇṇakaṅkho nimmāno, appameyyo anūpamo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbavākyapathātīto, sacca neyyantagū {note:sabbaneyyantiko (syā.)} jino.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattasāravare {pb:V:2.0109} {note:sataraṃsīvare (syā.)} tasmiṃ, pasādo amatāvaho;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā buddhe ca dhamme ca, saṅghe saddhā mahatthikā {note:mahiddhikā (sī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Guṇehi evamādīhi, tilokasaraṇuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇento parisāmajjhe, akaṃ {note:kathiṃ (syā.)} dhammakathaṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato cutāhaṃ tusite, anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato cuto manussesu, jāto homi sugandhiko.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nissāso mukhagandho ca, dehagandho tatheva me;
::

::gathalast
Sedagandho ca satataṃ, sabbagandhova hoti me {note:sabbagandhotiseti me (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mukhagandho {pb:T:2.0176} sadā mayhaṃ, padumuppalacampako;
::

::gathalast
Parisanto {note:ādisanto (sī.), atikanto (syā.), atisanto (pī.)} sadā vāti, sarīro ca tatheva me.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Guṇatthavassa sabbantaṃ, phalaṃ tu {note:phalantaṃ (syā.)} paramabbhutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekaggamanasā sabbe, vaṇṇayissaṃ {note:bhāsitassa (syā.)} suṇātha me.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Guṇaṃ {pb:P:2.0462} buddhassa vatvāna, hitāya ca na sadisaṃ {note:hitāya janasandhisu (sī. pī.), hitāya naṃ sukhāvahaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sukhito {note:sucitto (syā.)} homi sabbattha, saṅgho vīrasamāyuto {note:saraddhanisamāyuto (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yasassī sukhito kanto, jutimā piyadassano;
::

::gathalast
Vattā aparibhūto ca, niddoso paññavā tathā.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khīṇe āyusi {note:pāsusi (syā.)} nibbānaṃ, sulabhaṃ buddhabhattino;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ hetuṃ pavakkhāmi, taṃ suṇātha yathātathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Santaṃ {pb:M:2.0111} yasaṃ bhagavato, vidhinā abhivādayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha tatthūpapannopi {note:yattha tatthūpapannopi (sī. pī.)}, yasassī tena homahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkhassantakaraṃ buddhaṃ, dhammaṃ santamasaṅkhataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇayaṃ sukhado āsiṃ, sattānaṃ sukhito tato.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Guṇaṃ vadanto buddhassa, buddhapītisamāyuto;
::

::gathalast
Sakantiṃ parakantiñca, janayiṃ tena kantimā.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jino te titthikākiṇṇe {note:janoghe titthakākiṇṇe (sī. pī.), jino yo titthikātiṇṇo (syā.)}, abhibhuyya kutitthiye;
::

::gathalast
Guṇaṃ vadanto jotesiṃ {note:thomesiṃ (syā.)}, nāyakaṃ jutimā tato.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyakārī janassāpi, sambuddhassa guṇaṃ vadaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saradova sasaṅkohaṃ, tenāsiṃ piyadassano.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāsattivasenāhaṃ{pb:T:2.0177}{pb:V:2.0110}, sabbavācāhi santhaviṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sugataṃ tena vāgiso, vicittapaṭibhānavā.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye bālā vimatiṃ pattā, paribhonti mahāmuniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Niggahiṃ te saddhammena, paribhūto na tenahaṃ {note:paribhūtena tenahaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhavaṇṇena sattānaṃ, kilese apanesahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nikkilesamano homi, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sotūnaṃ {pb:P:2.0463} vuddhimajaniṃ {note:buddhimajaniṃ (sī. pī.)}, buddhānussatidesako;
::

::gathalast
Tenāhamāsiṃ {note:tenāpi cāsiṃ (syā.)} sappañño, nipuṇatthavipassako.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, tiṇṇasaṃsārasāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Sikhīva anupādāno, pāpuṇissāmi nibbutiṃ.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappasmiṃ, yamahaṃ santhaviṃ jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhavaṇṇassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:2.0112} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sugandho thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sugandhattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Tiṇadāyakavaggo tepaññāsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Tiṇado {pb:T:2.0178} mañcado ceva, saraṇabbhañjanappado;
::

::gathalast
Supaṭo daṇḍadāyī ca, nelapūjī tatheva ca.
::

::gatha1
Bodhisammajjako maṇḍo, sugandho dasamoti ca;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāsataṃ satevīsaṃ, gaṇitañcettha sabbaso.
::

### 54. Kaccāyanavaggo

#### 1. Mahākaccāyanattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0179}{pb:M:2.0113}{pb:V:2.0111} nāma jino, anejo ajitaṃ jayo;
::

::gathalast
Satasahasse kappānaṃ, ito uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīro kamalapattakkho, sasaṅkavimalānano;
::

::gathalast
Kanakācalasaṅkāso {note:kañcanatacasaṅkāso (syā.)}, ravidittisamappabho.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattanettamanohārī, varalakkhaṇabhūsito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbavākyapathātīto, manujāmarasakkato.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambuddho bodhayaṃ satte, vāgīso madhurassaro;
::

::gathalast
Karuṇānibandhasantāno, parisāsu visārado.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deseti {pb:P:2.0464} madhuraṃ dhammaṃ, catusaccūpasaṃhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nimugge mohapaṅkamhi, samuddharati pāṇine.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā ekacaro hutvā, tāpaso himavālayo;
::

::gathalast
Nabhasā mānusaṃ lokaṃ, gacchanto jinamaddasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upecca santikaṃ tassa, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇayantassa vīrassa, sāvakassa mahāguṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkhittena mayā vuttaṃ, vitthārena pakāsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parisaṃ mañca toseti, yathā kaccāyano ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nāhaṃ {pb:T:2.0180} evamidhekaccaṃ {note:evaṃvidhaṃ kañci (sī. pī.)}, aññaṃ passāmi sāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmātadagge {note:tasmetadagge (sī.)} esaggo, evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo’.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ vimhito hutvā, sutvā vākyaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Himavantaṃ gamitvāna, āhitvā {note:āhatvā (sī. pī.)} pupphasañcayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pūjetvā lokasaraṇaṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadā mamāsayaṃ ñatvā, byākāsi sa raṇañjaho.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Passathetaṃ {pb:V:2.0112} isivaraṃ, niddhantakanakattacaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uddhaggalomaṃ pīṇaṃsaṃ, acalaṃ pañjaliṃ ṭhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Hāsaṃ {pb:M:2.0114} supuṇṇanayanaṃ, buddhavaṇṇagatāsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhammajaṃ uggahadayaṃ {note:dhammaṃva viggahavaraṃ (sī.), dhammapaṭiggahavaraṃ (pī.)}, amatāsittasannibhaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaccānassa guṇaṃ sutvā, taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayaṃ ṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Anāgatamhi addhāne, gotamassa mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Kaccāno nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahussuto mahāñāṇī, adhippāyavidū mune;
::

::gathalast
Pāpuṇissati taṃ ṭhānaṃ, yathāyaṃ byākato mayā.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na gacchāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve {pb:T:2.0181} kule pajāyāmi, khattiye atha brāhmaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Nīce kule na jāyāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime {pb:P:2.0465} ca bhave dāni, jāto ujjeniyaṃ pure {note:jāto, ujjeniyaṃ pure rame (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Pajjotassa ca caṇḍassa, purohitadijādhino {note:purohitadijātino (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Putto tiriṭivacchassa {note:tiriṭavacchassa (sī.), tipitivacchassa (syā.)}, nipuṇo vedapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Mātā ca candimā nāma, kaccānohaṃ varattaco.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīmaṃsanatthaṃ buddhassa, bhūmipālena pesito;
::

::gathalast
Disvā mokkhapuradvāraṃ, nāyakaṃ guṇasañcayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvā ca vimalaṃ vākyaṃ, gatipaṅkavisosanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāpuṇiṃ amataṃ santaṃ, sesehi saha sattahi.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhippāyavidū jāto, sugatassa mahāmate;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhapito etadagge ca, susamiddhamanoratho.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:M:2.0115}{pb:V:2.0113} vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike; Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākaccāyano thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mahākaccāyanattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Vakkalittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:T:2.0182} satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Anomanāmo amito, nāmena padumuttaro.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumākāravadano, padumāmalasucchavī;
::

::gathalast
Lokenānupalittova toyena padumaṃ yathā.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīro padumapattakkho, kanto ca padumaṃ yathā;
::

::gathalast
Padumuttaragandhova, tasmā so padumuttaro.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lokajeṭṭho ca nimmāno, andhānaṃ nayanūpamo;
::

::gathalast
Santaveso guṇanidhi, karuṇāmatisāgaro.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa kadāci mahāvīro, brahmāsurasuraccito;
::

::gathalast
Sadevamanujākiṇṇe, janamajjhe jinuttamo {note:januttamo (syā. pī.), anuttamo (ka.) vaṅgīsattherāpadānepi}.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vadanena sugandhena, madhurena rutena ca;
::

::gathalast
Rañjayaṃ parisaṃ sabbaṃ, santhavī sāvakaṃ sakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhādhimutto {pb:P:2.0466} sumati, mama dassanalālaso {note:dassanasālayo (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Natthi etādiso añño, yathāyaṃ bhikkhu vakkali.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, nagare brāhmaṇatrajo;
::

::gathalast
Hutvā sutvā ca taṃ vākyaṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhirocayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sasāvakaṃ {pb:M:2.0116} taṃ vimalaṃ, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattāhaṃ bhojayitvāna, dussehacchādayiṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nipacca {pb:T:2.0183}{pb:V:2.0114} sirasā tassa, anantaguṇasāgare;
::

::gathalast
Nimuggo pītisampuṇṇo, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo so tayā santhavito, ito sattamake muni {note:idha saddhādhimutto isi (syā.), ito sattamakehani (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhu saddhāvataṃ aggo, tādiso homahaṃ mune’.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ vutte mahāvīro, anāvaraṇadassano;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ vākyaṃ udīresi, parisāya mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Passathetaṃ māṇavakaṃ, pītamaṭṭhanivāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hemayaññopacitaṅgaṃ {note:hemayaññopavītaṅgaṃ (sī.)}, jananettamanoharaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Eso anāgataddhāne, gotamassa mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Aggo saddhādhimuttānaṃ, sāvakoyaṃ bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devabhūto manusso vā, sabbasantāpavajjito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbabhogaparibyūḷho, sukhito saṃsarissati.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Vakkali nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammavisesena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbattha sukhito hutvā, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
::

::gathalast
Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto, kule aññatare ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nonītasukhumālaṃ {pb:T:2.0184} maṃ, jātapallavakomalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mandaṃ uttānasayanaṃ, pisācabhayatajjitā.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pādamūle mahesissa, sāyesuṃ dīnamānasā;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ dadāma te nātha, saraṇaṃ hohi nāyaka.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:M:2.0117}{pb:P:2.0467} paṭiggahi so maṃ, bhītānaṃ saraṇo muni;
::

::gathalast
Jālinā cakkaṅkitena {note:saṅkalaṅkena (sī.)}, mudukomalapāṇinā.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā pabhuti tenāhaṃ, arakkheyyena rakkhito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaveravinimutto {note:sabbabyādhivinimutto (syā.), sabbūpadhivinimutto (pī.)}, sukhena parivuddhito.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sugatena {pb:V:2.0115} vinā bhūto, ukkaṇṭhāmi muhuttakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbapāramisambhūtaṃ, nīlakkhinayanaṃ {note:laṅkinīlayanaṃ (sī.)} varaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rūpaṃ sabbasubhākiṇṇaṃ, atitto viharāmahaṃ {note:vihayāmahaṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddharūparatiṃ {note:buddho rūparatiṃ (sī.)} ñatvā, tadā ovadi maṃ jino;
::

::gathalast
‘Alaṃ vakkali kiṃ rūpe, ramase bālanandite.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo hi passati saddhammaṃ, so maṃ passati paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Apassamāno saddhammaṃ, maṃ passampi na passati.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Anantādīnavo kāyo, visarukkhasamūpamo;
::

::gathalast
Āvāso sabbarogānaṃ, puñjo dukkhassa kevalo.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nibbindiya tato rūpe, khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Passa upakkilesānaṃ, sukhenantaṃ gamissati’.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:T:2.0185} tenānusiṭṭhohaṃ, nāyakena hitesinā;
::

::gathalast
Gijjhakūṭaṃ samāruyha, jhāyāmi girikandare.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ṭhito pabbatapādamhi, assāsayi {note:mamāhaso (sī.)} mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Vakkalīti jino vācaṃ, taṃ sutvā mudito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pakkhandiṃ selapabbhāre, anekasataporise;
::

::gathalast
Tadā buddhānubhāvena, sukheneva mahiṃ gato.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Punopi {note:punāpi (syā.), muni maṃ (ka.)} dhammaṃ deseti, khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ dhammamaññāya, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumahāparisamajjhe{pb:M:2.0118}, tadā maṃ caraṇantago;
::

::gathalast
Aggaṃ saddhādhimuttānaṃ, paññapesi mahāmati.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:P:2.0468} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:2.0116} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vakkalitthero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Vakkalittherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Mahākappinattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0186} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Udito ajaṭākāse {note:jagadākāse (sī.), jaladākāse (pī.)}, ravīva saradambare.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vacanābhāya bodheti, veneyyapadumāni so;
::

::gathalast
Kilesapaṅkaṃ soseti, matiraṃsīhi nāyako.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Titthiyānaṃ yase {note:yaso (sī. pī.)} hanti, khajjotābhā yathā ravi;
::

Saccatthābhaṃ pakāseti, ratanaṃva divākaro.

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Guṇānaṃ āyatibhūto, ratanānaṃva sāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Pajjunnoriva bhūtāni, dhammameghena vassati.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhadasso tadā āsiṃ, nagare haṃsasavhaye;
::

::gathalast
Upecca dhammamassosiṃ, jalajuttamanāmino.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ovādakassa bhikkhūnaṃ, sāvakassa katāvino;
::

::gathalast
Guṇaṃ pakāsayantassa, tappayantassa {note:tosayantassa (sī.), hāsayantassa (syā.), vāsayantassa (pī.)} me manaṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvā patīto sumano, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sasissaṃ bhojayitvāna, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:M:2.0119} haṃsasamabhāgo, haṃsadundubhinissano {note:haṃsadundubhisussaro (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Passathetaṃ mahāmattaṃ, vinicchayavisāradaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parivārena {pb:T:2.0187} mahatā, rājayuttaṃ mahāyasaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iminā {pb:V:2.0117}{pb:P:2.0469} paṇipātena, cāgena paṇidhīhi ca {note:piṇḍapātena, cetanā paṇidhīhi ca (sī.)};

::gathalast

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1

78\.

::hangnum
80\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
81\.

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
83\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
84\.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Kukkuṭamhi pure jātā, himavantassa passato.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
87\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

::gatha1

::gathalast

‘‘Vanditvāna sahāmacco, ekamantamupāvisiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato no āsayaṃ {note:tato ajjhāsayaṃ (syā.)} ñatvā, buddho dhammamadesayi.

::hangnum
98\.

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvāna {pb:M:2.0121} dhammaṃ vimalaṃ, avocumha mayaṃ jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast

#### 4. Dabbamallaputtattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:P:2.0471} nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anukampako {pb:M:2.0122} kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi {note:patiṭṭhahi (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ {note:suññakaṃ (sī.) evamuparipi} titthiyehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ, uggato so mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni{pb:T:2.0191}, āyu vijjati tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Upetvā lokapajjotaṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Senāsanāni bhikkhūnaṃ, paññāpentaṃ sasāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kittayantassa vacanaṃ, suṇitvā mudito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhikāraṃ {pb:V:2.0120} sasaṅghassa, katvā tassa mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Nipacca sirasā pāde, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāha sa mahāvīro, mama kammaṃ pakittayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘Yo sasaṅghamabhojesi, sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Soyaṃ kamalapattakkho, sīhaṃso kanakattaco;
::

::gathalast
Mama pādamūle nipati {note:patito (pī.)}, patthayaṃ ṭhānamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Senāsanapaññāpako, aggo hessatiyaṃ tadā’.

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1

122\.

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ {pb:T:2.0192}{pb:M:2.0123}{pb:P:2.0472} vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.

::hangnum
124\.

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, vipassī nāma nāyako;

126\.

::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
129\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
130\.

::hangnum
131\.

134\.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addasamha {pb:M:2.0124} tadāraññe, ubbiddhaṃ selamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:P:2.0473} ovadi no thero, buddhuppādo sudullabho;

::gathalast

::hangnum
138\.

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Arahā āsi so thero, anāgāmī tadānugo;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Saṃsārabandhanā muttā, gotamenānukampitā.

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
144\.

::gatha1

145\.

146\.

#### 5. Kumārakassapattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:M:2.0125} satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Sabbalokahito vīro, padumuttaranāmako.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ {pb:T:2.0195} brāhmaṇo hutvā, vissuto vedapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Divāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
152\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catusaccaṃ {pb:P:2.0474} pakāsentaṃ, bodhayantaṃ sadevakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vicittakathikānaggaṃ, vaṇṇayantaṃ mahājane.
::

::hangnum
153\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā muditacittohaṃ, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānārattehi vatthehi, alaṅkaritvāna maṇḍapaṃ.
::

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nānāratanapajjotaṃ, sasaṅghaṃ bhojayiṃ tahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhojayitvāna sattāhaṃ, nānaggarasabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nānācittehi {note:nānāvaṇṇehi (sī.)} pupphehi, pūjayitvā sasāvakaṃ {note:mahāvīraṃ (ka.)};

::hangnum

#### 6. Bāhiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
178\.

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:T:2.0198} satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Mahappabho tilokaggo, nāmena padumuttaro.
::

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khippābhiññassa bhikkhussa, guṇaṃ kittayato mune;

::gathalast

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Datvā sattāhikaṃ dānaṃ, sasissassa mune ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
181\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Patitaṃ pādamūle me, cariyaṃ paccavekkhaṇaṃ {note:pasannanayanānanaṃ (sī.), pīnasampannavekkhaṇaṃ (syā.), pīṇaṃsaṃ paccavekkhaṇaṃ (pī.)}.

#### 7. Mahākoṭṭhikattheraapadānaṃ

222\.

228\.

::gatha1

232\.

::gatha1
‘‘Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
239\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
::

::hangnum
240\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve {pb:T:2.0205} bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na gacchāmi, suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
241\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve kule pajāyāmi, khattiye atha brāhmaṇe;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Nīce kule na jāyāmi, suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
242\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, brahmabandhu ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāvatthiyaṃ vippakule, paccājāto mahaddhane.
::

::hangnum
243\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātā candavatī nāma, pitā me assalāyano;
::

::gathalast
Yadā me pitaraṃ buddho, vinayī sabbasuddhiyā.
::

::hangnum
244\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:M:2.0133} pasanno sugate, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Moggallāno ācariyo, upajjhā sārisambhavo.
::

::hangnum
245\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kesesu chijjamānesu, diṭṭhi chinnā samūlikā;
::

::gathalast
Nivāsento ca kāsāvaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
246\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne ca me mati;
::

::gathalast
Pabhinnā tena lokaggo, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
247\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asandiṭṭhaṃ viyākāsiṃ, upatissena pucchito;
::

::gathalast

::

248\.

::gatha1

::

#### 8. Uruveḷakassapattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
251\.

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:V:2.0130}{pb:P:2.0481} nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.

::hangnum
252\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
253\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
254\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
255\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
257\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
258\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:T:2.0207} mahāparisatiṃ, mahāparisasāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhapentaṃ etadaggamhi, sutvāna mudito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
259\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
260\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, abhivādiya nāyakaṃ;
::

::hangnum
261\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
262\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

#### 10. Mogharājattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
327\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.
::

::hangnum
328\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
329\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi.
::

::hangnum
330\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ titthiyehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
::

::hangnum
331\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ{pb:M:2.0140}, uggato so mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
::

::hangnum
332\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni{pb:V:2.0136}, āyu vijjati tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
333\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ {pb:T:2.0215} haṃsavatiyaṃ, kule aññatare ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parakammāyane yutto, natthi me kiñci saṃdhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
334\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ, vasanto katabhūmiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggiṃ ujjālayiṃ tattha, daḷhaṃ kaṇhāsi sā {note:kaṇhā siyā (sī. pī.), ḍayhakaṇhā silā (syā.)} hī.
::

::hangnum
335\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā parisatiṃ nātho, catusaccapakāsako;
::

::gathalast
Sāvakaṃ sampakittesi, lūkhacīvaradhārakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
336\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho, paṇipacca {note:patipajja (syā.)} tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lūkhacīvaradhāraggaṃ, patthayiṃ ṭhānamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
337\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā avoca bhagavā, sāvake padumuttaro;
::

::gathalast
‘Passathetaṃ purisakaṃ, kucelaṃ tanudehakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
338\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Pītippasannavadanaṃ{pb:P:2.0487}, saddhādhanasamanvitaṃ {note:saddhāsnehasamanvataṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Udaggatanujaṃ haṭṭhaṃ, acalaṃ sālapiṇḍitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
339\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Eso pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ, saccasenassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Lūkhacīvaradhārissa, tassa vaṇṇasitāsayo {note:vaṇṇagatāsayo (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
340\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā, nipacca sirasā jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yāvajīvaṃ subhaṃ kammaṃ, karitvā jinasāsane.
::

::hangnum
341\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsūpago ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
342\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ, bhūmidāhakakammunā;
::

::gathalast
Samasahassaṃ niraye, adayhiṃ vedanāṭṭito.
::

::hangnum
343\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:2.0216} kammāvasesena, pañca jātisatānihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manusso kulajo hutvā, jātiyā lakkhaṇaṅkito.
::

::hangnum
344\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca {pb:M:2.0141} jātisatāneva, kuṭṭharogasamappito;
::

::gathalast
Mahādukkhaṃ anubhaviṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
::

::hangnum
345\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe, upariṭṭhaṃ yasassinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piṇḍapātena tappesiṃ, pasannamānaso ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
346\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:V:2.0137} kammavisesena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
347\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, ajāyiṃ khattiye kule;
::

::gathalast
Pituno accayenāhaṃ, mahārajjasamappito.
::

::hangnum
348\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṭṭharogādhibhūtohaṃ, na ratiṃ na sukhaṃ labhe;
::

::gathalast
Moghaṃ rajjaṃ sukhaṃ yasmā, mogharājā tato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
349\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāyassa dosaṃ disvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bāvarissa dijaggassa, sissattaṃ ajjhupāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
350\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahatā parivārena, upecca naranāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Apucchiṃ nipuṇaṃ pañhaṃ, taṃ vīraṃ vādisūdanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
351\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ayaṃ loko paro loko, brahmaloko sadevako;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭhiṃ no {note:diṭṭhā no (sī.), diṭṭhaṃ no (pī.), diṭṭhiṃ te (syā.)} nābhijānāmi, gotamassa yasassino.
::

::hangnum
352\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Evābhikkantadassāviṃ{pb:P:2.0488}, atthi pañhena āgamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ, maccurājā na passati’.
::

::hangnum
353\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Suññato {pb:T:2.0217} lokaṃ avekkhassu, mogharāja sadā sato;
::

::gathalast
Attānudiṭṭhiṃ uhacca, evaṃ maccutaro siyā.
::

::hangnum
354\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Evaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ, maccurājā na passati’;
::

::gathalast
Iti maṃ abhaṇi buddho, sabbarogatikicchako.
::

::hangnum
355\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saha gāthāvasānena, kesamassuvivajjito;
::

::gathalast
Kāsāvavatthavasano, āsiṃ bhikkhu tathārahā.
::

::hangnum
356\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅghikesu vihāresu, na vasiṃ rogapīḷito;
::

::gathalast
Mā vihāro padussīti, vātarogehi pīḷito {note:vācāyābhisupīḷito (syā. pī.), vātarogī supīḷito (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
357\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkārakūṭā {pb:M:2.0142} āhitvā, susānā rathikāhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Tato saṅghāṭiṃ karitvā, dhārayiṃ lūkhacīvaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
358\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahābhisakko tasmiṃ me, guṇe tuṭṭho vināyako;
::

::gathalast
Lūkhacīvaradhārīnaṃ, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
359\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puññapāpaparikkhīṇo, sabbarogavivajjito;
::

::gathalast
Sikhīva anupādāno, nibbāyissamanāsavo.
::

::hangnum
360\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0138} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
361\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
362\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0218} sudaṃ āyasmā mogharājā thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mogharājattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kaccāyanavaggo catupaññāsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kaccāno vakkalī thero, mahākappinasavhayo;
::

::gathalast
Dabbo kumāranāmo ca, bāhiyo koṭṭhiko vasī.
::

::gatha1
Uruveḷakassapo rādho, mogharājā ca paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Tīṇi gāthāsatānettha, bāsaṭṭhi ceva piṇḍitā.
::

### 55. Bhaddiyavaggo

#### 1. Lakuṇḍabhaddiyattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0219}{pb:M:2.0143}{pb:V:2.0139}{pb:P:2.0489} nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, seṭṭhiputto mahaddhano;
::

::gathalast
Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ, saṅghārāmaṃ agacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā so lokapajjoto, dhammaṃ desesi nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Mañjussarānaṃ pavaraṃ, sāvakaṃ abhikittayi.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā, kāraṃ katvā mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā buddho viyākāsi, saṅghamajjhe vināyako;
::

::gathalast
‘Anāgatamhi addhāne, lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Bhaddiyo nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute {pb:T:2.0220} ito kappe, phusso uppajji nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Durāsado duppasaho, sabbalokuttamo jino.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Caraṇena ca sampanno, brahā uju patāpavā;
::

::gathalast
Hitesī sabbasattānaṃ {note:sabbapāṇīnaṃ (sī.)}, bahuṃ mocesi bandhanā.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandārāmavane tassa, ahosiṃ phussakokilo {note:pussakokilo (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Gandhakuṭisamāsanne, ambarukkhe vasāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:V:2.0140} piṇḍāya gacchantaṃ, dakkhiṇeyyaṃ jinuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā, mañjunābhinikūjahaṃ {note:mañjunādena kūjahaṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājuyyānaṃ {pb:M:2.0144} tadā gantvā, supakkaṃ kanakattacaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ambapiṇḍaṃ gahetvāna, sambuddhassopanāmayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā me cittamaññāya, mahākāruṇiko jino;
::

::gathalast
Upaṭṭhākassa hatthato, pattaṃ paggaṇhi nāyako.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adāsiṃ {pb:P:2.0490} haṭṭhacittohaṃ {note:tuṭṭhacittohaṃ (sī.)}, ambapiṇḍaṃ mahāmune;
::

::gathalast
Patte pakkhippa pakkhehi, pañjaliṃ {note:pakkhehañjaliṃ (sī.)} katvāna mañjunā.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sarena rajanīyena, savanīyena vaggunā;
::

::gathalast
Vassanto buddhapūjatthaṃ, nīḷaṃ {note:niddaṃ (syā. pī.)} gantvā nipajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā muditacittaṃ maṃ, buddhapemagatāsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakuṇagghi upāgantvā, ghātayī duṭṭhamānaso.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato cutohaṃ tusite, anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manussayonimāgacchiṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imamhi {pb:T:2.0221} bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāsanaṃ jotayitvā so, abhibhuyya kutitthiye;
::

::gathalast
Vinayitvāna veneyye, nibbuto so sasāvako.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbute tamhi lokagge, pasannā janatā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Pūjanatthāya buddhassa, thūpaṃ kubbanti satthuno.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sattayojanikaṃ thūpaṃ, sattaratanabhūsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Karissāma mahesissa’, iccevaṃ mantayanti te.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kikino kāsirājassa, tadā senāya nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Hutvāhaṃ appamāṇassa, pamāṇaṃ cetiye vadiṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā te mama vākyena, cetiyaṃ yojanuggataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akaṃsu naravīrassa, nānāratanabhūsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime {pb:M:2.0145}{pb:V:2.0141} ca bhave dāni, jāto seṭṭhikule ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purappavese sugataṃ, disvā vimhitamānaso;
::

::gathalast
Pabbajitvāna na ciraṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cetiyassa pamāṇaṃ yaṃ, akariṃ tena kammunā;
::

::gathalast
Lakuṇḍakasarīrohaṃ, jāto paribhavāraho.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sarena {pb:T:2.0222} madhurenāhaṃ, pūjitvā isisattamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mañjussarānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, aggattamanupāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phaladānena {pb:P:2.0491} buddhassa, guṇānussaraṇena ca;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaññaphalasampanno, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lakuṇḍabhaddiyo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Lakuṇḍabhaddiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Kaṅkhārevatattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīhahanu brahmagiro, haṃsadundubhinissano {note:haṃsadundubhinissaro (sī.) … nissavano (pī.) … sāvano (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Nāgavikkantagamano, candasūrādikappabho.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāmatī {pb:M:2.0146} mahāvīro, mahājhāyī mahābalo {note:mahāgati (syā.), mahāhito (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Mahākāruṇiko nātho, mahātamapanūdano {note:mahātamavidhaṃsano (syā.), mahātamanisūdano (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa {pb:T:2.0223}{pb:V:2.0142} kadāci tilokaggo, veneyyaṃ vinayaṃ bahuṃ {note:veneyye viniyaṃ bahū (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ desesi sambuddho, sattāsayavidū muni.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ vīraṃ, upasantaṃ anāvilaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇayanto parisatiṃ, tosesi {note:toseti (syā. pī. ka.)} janataṃ jino.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, brāhmaṇo vedapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ sutvāna mudito, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā jino viyākāsi, saṅghamajjhe vināyako;
::

::gathalast
‘Mudito hohi tvaṃ brahme, lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Revato nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātohaṃ koliye pure;
::

::gathalast
Khattiye kulasampanne, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā {pb:P:2.0492} kapilavatthusmiṃ, buddho dhammamadesayi;
::

::gathalast
Tadā pasanno sugate, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṅkhā me bahulā āsi, kappākappe tahiṃ tahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ taṃ vinayī buddho, desetvā dhammamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatohaṃ {pb:T:2.0224} tiṇṇasaṃsāro, sadā jhānasukhe rato;
::

::gathalast
Viharāmi tadā buddho, maṃ disvā etadabravi.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yā {pb:M:2.0147} kāci kaṅkhā idha vā huraṃ vā, sakavediyā vā paravediyā vā;
::

::gathalast
Ye jhāyino tā pajahanti sabbā, ātāpino brahmacariyaṃ carantā’.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
::

::gathalast
Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayiṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato jhānarataṃ disvā, buddho lokantagū muni;
::

::gathalast
Jhāyīnaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ aggo, paññāpeti mahāmati.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0143} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kaṅkhārevato thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Kaṅkhārevatattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Sīvalittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0225} nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīlaṃ tassa asaṅkheyyaṃ, samādhi vajirūpamo;
::

::gathalast
Asaṅkheyyaṃ ñāṇavaraṃ, vimutti ca anopamā.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manujāmaranāgānaṃ, brahmānañca samāgame;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇabrāhmaṇākiṇṇe, dhammaṃ desesi nāyako.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sasāvakaṃ mahālābhiṃ, puññavantaṃ jutindharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi, parisāsu visārado.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ khattiyo āsiṃ, nagare haṃsasavhaye;
::

::gathalast
Sutvā jinassa taṃ vākyaṃ, sāvakassa guṇaṃ bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nimantayitvā {pb:M:2.0148}{pb:P:2.0493} sattāhaṃ, bhojayitvā sasāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā maṃ vinataṃ pāde, disvāna purisāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Sarena mahatā vīro {note:sussarena mahāvīro (sī. pī.)}, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tato jinassa vacanaṃ, sotukāmā mahājanā;
::

::gathalast
Devadānavagandhabbā, brahmāno ca mahiddhikā’.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇabrāhmaṇā ceva, namassiṃsu katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
‘Namo te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Khattiyena {pb:T:2.0226}{pb:V:2.0144} mahādānaṃ, dinnaṃ sattāhikampi vo {note:sattahikaṃ mi vo (sī.), sattahikādhikaṃ (syā.), sattahikaṃ vibho (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sotukāmā phalaṃ tassa, byākarohi mahāmune’.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato avoca bhagavā, ‘suṇātha mama bhāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appameyyamhi buddhamhi, sasaṅghamhi patiṭṭhitā {note:saṃghamhi suppatiṭṭhitā (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dakkhiṇā tāya {note:dakkhiṇādāya (syā. pī.)} ko vattā, appameyyaphalā hi sā;
::

::gathalast
Api ce sa mahābhogo, ṭhānaṃ pattheti uttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Lābhī vipulalābhānaṃ, yathā bhikkhu sudassano;
::

::gathalast
Tathāhampi bhaveyyanti, lacchase taṃ anāgate.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sīvali nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsūpago ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, vipassī lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Uppajji cārudassano, sabbadhammavipassako.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ {pb:M:2.0149} bandhumatiyaṃ, kulassaññatarassa ca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā aññataro pūgo, vipassissa mahesino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Niṭṭhite {pb:T:2.0227}{pb:P:2.0494} ca mahādāne, daduṃ khajjakasañhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Navaṃ dadhiṃ madhuñceva, vicinaṃ neva addasuṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassamapi datvāna, nālabhiṃsu ca taṃ dvayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatohaṃ evaṃ cintesiṃ, ‘netaṃ hessati orakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yathā ime janā sabbe, sakkaronti tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi kāraṃ kassāmi, sasaṅghe lokanāyake’.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhamevaṃ {pb:V:2.0145} cintetvā, dadhiṃ madhuñca ekato;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
79\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā tapassino ruddhā, ekāhaṃ rakkhitā ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato tassa vipākena, pāpatiṃ {note:pāpiṭṭhaṃ (syā.) pāpattaṃ (ka.)} nirayaṃ bhusaṃ.

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātohaṃ koliye pure;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khattiye puññakammena, dvārarodhassa vāhasā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
84\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
85\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
87\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
89\.

::gathalast

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gathalast

#### 4. Vaṅgīsattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi {pb:M:2.0151} sāgare ūmi, gagane viya tārakā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ pāvacanaṃ tassa, arahantehi cittitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sadevāsuranāgehi, manujehi purakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇabrāhmaṇākiṇṇe, janamajjhe jinuttamo.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhāhi anurañjanto, loke {note:lokaṃ (sī.)} lokantagū jino;
::

::gathalast
Vacanena vibodhento, veneyyapadumāni so.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vesārajjehi sampanno, catūhi purisuttamo;
::

::gathalast
Pahīnabhayasārajjo, khemappatto visārado.

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsabhaṃ {pb:T:2.0230}{pb:P:2.0496} pavaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, buddhabhūmiñca kevalaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīhanādamasambhītaṃ, nadato tassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Devo naro vā brahmā vā, paṭivattā na vijjati.

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Desento {pb:V:2.0147} pavaraṃ dhammaṃ, santārento sadevakaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭibhānavataṃ aggaṃ, sāvakaṃ sādhusammataṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, brāhmaṇo sādhusammato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbavedavidū jāto, vāgīso vādisūdano.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upecca taṃ mahāvīraṃ, sutvāhaṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pītivaraṃ paṭilabhiṃ, sāvakassa guṇe rato.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nimantetvāva sugataṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanandanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattāhaṃ bhojayitvāhaṃ, dussehacchādayiṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nipacca sirasā pāde, katokāso katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Ekamantaṃ ṭhito haṭṭho, santhaviṃ jinamuttamaṃ.

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Namo te vādimaddana {note:vādisaddula (sī. pī.), vādisūdana (syā.)}, namo te isisattama {note:purisuttama (sī. pī.)};

::gathalast

110\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Anāthānaṃ {pb:T:2.0231} bhavaṃ nātho, bhītānaṃ abhayappado;
::

::gathalast
Vissāmabhūmi {note:vissāsaṃ bhūmi (syā.), vissānabhūmi (pī.)} santānaṃ, saraṇaṃ saraṇesinaṃ’.

112\.

113\.

114\.

::hangnum
124\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast
Kaṇikāraṃva nicitaṃ {note:kaṇikāraparicitaṃ (pī.), khaṇikaṃ ṭhānaracitaṃ (sī.)}, cittaṃ gāthāpadaṃ ahaṃ.

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Virāgasaṃhitaṃ vākyaṃ, katvā duddasamuttamaṃ;

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nipacca sirasā pāde, ‘pabbājehī’ti maṃ bravi;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
129\.

::gatha1
‘‘Nipacca sirasā pāde, nisīdiṃ satthu santike;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
130\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gathalast

131\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā khīṇāsavasseva {note:paccekabuddhassa (sī. pī.)}, sīsaṃ dassesi nāyako;
::

::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbajitvāna sugataṃ, santhavāmi tahiṃ tahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato maṃ kabbavittosi {note:kavicittoti (syā. pī.)}, ujjhāyantiha bhikkhavo.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:2.0154} vīmaṃsanatthaṃ me, āha buddho vināyako;
::

::gathalast
Takkikā panimā gāthā, ṭhānaso paṭibhanti taṃ.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na kabbavittohaṃ vīra, ṭhānaso paṭibhanti maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena hi dāni vaṅgīsa, ṭhānaso santhavāhi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ santhaviṃ vīraṃ, gāthāhi isisattamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhānaso me tadā tuṭṭho, jino agge ṭhapesi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭibhānena cittena, aññesamatimaññahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pesale tena saṃviggo, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paṭibhānavataṃ aggo, añño koci na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Yathāyaṃ bhikkhu vaṅgīso, evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo’.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
::

::gathalast
Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayiṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:T:2.0234} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum

#### 5. Nandakattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum

150\.
::

221\.

::gatha1
‘‘Abhitthavitvā padumuttarāhaṃ, pasannacitto asamaṃ sayambhuṃ;

::gathalast
Na gacchi kappāni apāyabhūmiṃ, sataṃ sahassāni balena tassa.

::centre

::

::centre
Bhaddiyavaggo pañcapaññāsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:M:2.0168} –

::gatha1
Bhaddiyo revato thero, mahālābhī ca sīvalī;
::

::gathalast
Vaṅgīso nandako ceva, kāḷudāyī tathābhayo.
::

::gatha1
Lomaso vanavaccho ca, sugandho ceva dasamo;
::

::gathalast
Tīṇi gāthāsatā tattha, soḷasā ca taduttari.
::

Atha {pb:V:2.0163} vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kaṇikāravhayo vaggo, phalado tiṇadāyako;
::

::gathalast
Kaccāno bhaddiyo vaggo, gāthāyo gaṇitā cimā.
::

::gatha1
Navagāthāsatānīha{pb:T:2.0253}{pb:P:2.0511}, caturāsītiyeva ca;
::

::gathalast
Sapaññāsaṃ pañcasataṃ, apadānā pakāsitā.
::

::gatha1
Saha udānagāthāhi, chasahassāni hontimā;
::

::gathalast
Dvesatāni ca gāthānaṃ, aṭṭhārasa taduttari.
::

### 56. Yasavaggo

#### 1. Yasattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāsamuddaṃ {pb:M:2.0169}{pb:V:2.0164} oggayha, bhavanaṃ me sunimmitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sunimmitā pokkharaṇī, cakkavākūpakūjitā.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mandārakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Nadī ca sandate tattha, supatitthā manoramā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Macchakacchapasañchannā, nānādijasamotthaṭā {note:nānāmigasamotthaṭā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Mayūrakoñcābhirudā, kokilādīhi vagguhi.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pārevatā ravihaṃsā, cakkavākā nadīcarā;
::

::gathalast
Tittirā sāḷikā cettha, pāvakā {note:sambakā (ka.)} jīvaṃjīvakā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Haṃsākoñcābhinaditā, kosiyā piṅgalā {note:piṅgalī (sī.), siṅgalī, siṅghalī (ka.)} bahū;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanasampannā, maṇimuttapavāḷikā.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe soṇṇamayā rukkhā, nānākhandhasameritā;
::

::gathalast
Ujjotenti divārattiṃ, bhavanaṃ sabbakālikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni, sāyaṃ pāto pavajjare;
::

::gathalast
Soḷasitthisahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhinikkhamma bhavanā, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto sumano, vandayiṃ taṃ {note:sabbadassiṃ (ka.)} mahāyasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, sasaṅghaṃ taṃ nimantayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adhivāsesi so dhīro, sumedho lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mama dhammakathaṃ katvā, uyyojesi mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, bhavanaṃ me upāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āmantayiṃ parijanaṃ, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
‘Pubbaṇhasamayaṃ buddho, bhavanaṃ āgamissati’.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Lābhā {pb:M:2.0170} amhaṃ suladdhā no, ye vasāma tavantike;
::

::gathalast
Mayampi buddhaseṭṭhassa, pūjayissāma satthuno’.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annaṃ {pb:V:2.0165} pānaṃ paṭṭhapetvā, kālaṃ ārocayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vasīsatasahassehi, upesi lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcaṅgikehi turiyehi, paccuggamamakāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbasoṇṇamaye pīṭhe, nisīdi purisuttamo.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uparicchadanaṃ āsi, sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Bījanīyo pavāyanti, bhikkhusaṅghaṃ anuttaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahūtenannapānena, bhikkhusaṅghaṃ atappayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paccekadussayugale, bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ vadeti sumedho so, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo maṃ annena pānena, sabbe ime ca tappayi;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, devaloke ramissati;
::

::gathalast
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājāyaṃ, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Upagacchati yaṃ yoniṃ, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ tassa, chadanaṃ dhārayissati.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, sīhanādaṃ nadissati’;
::

::gathalast
Citake chattaṃ dhārenti, heṭṭhā chattamhi ḍayhatha.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāmaññaṃ me anuppattaṃ, kilesā jhāpitā mayā;
::

::gathalast
Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, santāso me na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:M:2.0171} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:2.0166} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā yaso thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Yasattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Nadīkassapattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarassa bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gatha2
Piṇḍacāraṃ carantassa, vārato uttamaṃ yasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggaphalaṃ gahetvāna, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena devindo, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
::

::gathalast
Sampattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, aggadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nadīkassapo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Nadīkassapattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

43\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Aññe devetirocāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Channo salalapupphehi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.

#### 6. Uttarattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Vivekakāmo bhagavā, himavantamupāgami.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā himavantaṃ, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
::

::gathalast
Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna, nisīdi purisuttamo.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vijjadharo {pb:M:2.0174} tadā āsiṃ, antalikkhacaro ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tisūlaṃ sugataṃ gayha, gacchāmi ambare tadā.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbatagge yathā aggi, puṇṇamāyeva candimā;
::

::gathalast
Vanaṃ obhāsate buddho, sālarājāva phullito.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanaggā nikkhamitvāna, buddharaṃsībhidhāvare {note:buddharaṃsī vidhāvare (sī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Naḷaggivaṇṇasaṅkāsā {note:naḷaggiva nasaṅkāsaṃ (sī.)}, disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vicinaṃ addasaṃ pupphaṃ, kaṇikāraṃ devagandhikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tīṇi pupphāni ādāya, buddhaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhassa ānubhāvena, tīṇi pupphāni me tadā;
::

::gathalast
Uddhaṃ vaṇṭā adhopattā, chāyaṃ kubbanti satthuno.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, kaṇikārīti {note:kaṇikāroti (sī.)} ñāyati;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassakaṇḍaṃ {pb:V:2.0169} satabheṇḍu, dhajālu haritāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satasahassaniyyūhā {note:satasahassāni byūhāni (sī.)}, byamhe pātubhaviṃsu {note:pāturahaṃsu (sī.), pāturahiṃsu (ka.)} me.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soṇṇamayā maṇimayā, lohitaṅkamayāpi ca;
::

::gathalast
Phalikāpi ca pallaṅkā, yenicchakā yadicchakā.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahārahañca sayanaṃ, tūlikā vikatīyutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uddhalomiñca ekantaṃ, bimbohanasamāyutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavanā nikkhamitvāna, caranto devacārikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yathā icchāmi {note:yathā gacchāmi (sī.)} gamanaṃ, devasaṅghapurakkhato.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphassa heṭṭhā tiṭṭhāmi, uparicchadanaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Samantā yojanasataṃ, kaṇikārehi chāditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni{pb:M:2.0175}, sāyapātaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ, rattindivamatanditā.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha naccehi gītehi, tālehi vāditehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Ramāmi khiḍḍā ratiyā, modāmi kāmakāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, modāmi tidase tadā;
::

::gathalast
Nārīgaṇehi sahito, modāmi byamhamuttame.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhave bhave saṃsaranto, mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duve kule pajāyāmi {note:yattha pacchā pajāyāmi (sī.)}, khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Nīce kule na jāyāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, sivikaṃ sandamānikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dāsīgaṇaṃ dāsagaṇaṃ, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koseyyakambaliyāni, khomakappāsikāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Navavatthaṃ {pb:V:2.0170} navaphalaṃ, navaggarasabhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imaṃ khāda imaṃ bhuñja, imamhi sayane saya;
::

::gathalast
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbattha pūjito homi, yaso accuggato mama;
::

::gatha2
Mahāpakkho {note:mahesakkho (ka.)} sadā homi, abhejjapariso sadā;
::

::gathalast
Ñātīnaṃ uttamo homi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sītaṃ {pb:M:2.0176} uṇhaṃ na jānāmi, pariḷāho na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Atho cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ, hadaye me na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo hutvāna, saṃsarāmi bhavābhave;
::

::gathalast
Vevaṇṇiyaṃ na jānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto, mahāsālesu aḍḍhake.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upasampadāyī buddho, guṇamaññāya cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Taruṇo pūjanīyohaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbacakkhuvisuddhaṃ me, samādhikusalo ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhiññāpāramippatto, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā anuppatto, iddhipādesu kovido;
::

::gathalast
Dhammesu pāramippatto, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uttaro thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Uttarattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 8. Bhaddajittheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ogayha yaṃ pokkharaṇiṃ, nānākuñjarasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uddharāmi bhisaṃ tattha, ghāsahetu ahaṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, padumuttarasavhayo;
::

::gathalast
Rattambaradharo buddho, gacchate anilañjase.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhunanto paṃsukūlāni, saddaṃ assosahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Uddhaṃ nijjhāyamānohaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattheva ṭhitako santo, āyāciṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Madhuṃ bhisehi sahitaṃ, khīraṃ sappiṃ muḷālikaṃ {note:madhuṃ bhisehi pacati, khīrasappi mulālibhi (ka.) bhisadāyakattherāpadānepi}.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggaṇhātu me buddho, anukampāya cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggaṇhi mama bhikkhaṃ, anukampāya cakkhumā;
::

::hangnum
104\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
105\.

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato bhisaṃ gahetvāna, agacchiṃ mama assamaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

#### 10. Upavānattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
122\.

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahājanā samāgamma, pūjayitvā tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
126\.

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha pañcamikā ceva {note:tattha pañcamikā ceti (sī.)}, lohitaṅkamayā ahu;

::gathalast

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
128\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
129\.

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

132\.

152\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

153\.

154\.

155\.

::

#### 11. Raṭṭhapālattheraapadānaṃ

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarassa {pb:V:2.0177} bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Varanāgo mayā dinno, īsādanto urūḷhavā.
::

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Setacchattopasobhito, sakappano {note:sīdabbano (sī.)} sahatthipo;
::

::gathalast
Agghāpetvāna taṃ sabbaṃ, saṅghārāmaṃ akārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
181\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catupaññāsasahassāni, pāsāde kārayiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahoghadānaṃ {note:mahagghañca (sī.), mayā bhattaṃ (ka.) apa. thera 1.2.99} karitvāna, niyyādesiṃ mahesino.
::

::hangnum
182\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anumodi {pb:M:2.0184} mahāvīro, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe jane hāsayanto, desesi amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me buddho viyākāsi, jalajuttamanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Catupaññāsasahassāni, pāsāde kārayī ayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kathayissāmi vipākaṃ, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārasasahassāni, kūṭāgārā bhavissare;
::

::gathalast
Byamhuttamamhi nibbattā, sabbasoṇṇamayā ca te.
::

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Aḍḍhe kule mahābhoge, nibbattissati tāvade.
::

::hangnum
189\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhapāloti nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
::

::hangnum
190\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Padhānapahitatto so, upasanto nirūpadhi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhāya abhinikkhamma, jahitā bhogasampadā;
::

::gathalast
Kheḷapiṇḍeva bhogamhi, pemaṃ mayhaṃ na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
::

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0178} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
::

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:2.0185} catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā raṭṭhapālo thero imā gāthāyo
::

Abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Raṭṭhapālattherassāpadānaṃ ekādasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Yasavaggo chapaññāsamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Yaso nadīkassapo ca, gayākimilavajjino;
::

::gatha2
Duve uttarā bhaddajī, sivako upavāhano;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhapālo ekasataṃ, gāthānaṃ pañcanavuti.
::

::centre
Therāpadānaṃ samattaṃ.
::

::centre
Ettāvatā buddhāpadānañca paccekāpadānañca therāpadānañca
::

Samattāni.

::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Khuddakanikāye

## Therīapadānapāḷi

### 1. Sumedhāvaggo

#### 1. Sumedhātherīapadānaṃ

Atha therikāpadānāni suṇātha –

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhagavati {pb:T:2.0254}{pb:M:2.0187}{pb:V:2.0179}{pb:P:2.0512} koṇāgamane, saṅghārāmamhi navanivesanamhi {note:nivesamhi (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sakhiyo tisso janiyo, vihāradānaṃ adāsimha.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dasakkhattuṃ satakkhattuṃ, dasasatakkhattuṃ satānañca satakkhattuṃ {note:satāni ca sattakkhattuṃ (sī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Devesu upapajjimha, ko vādo mānuse bhave.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deve {pb:V:2.0180} mahiddhikā ahumha, mānusakamhi ko vādo;
::

::gathalast
Sattaratanamahesī {note:sattaratanassa mahesī (sī. pī.)}, itthiratanaṃ ahaṃ bhaviṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idha sañcitakusalā {note:tattha sañcitaṃ kusalaṃ (syā.)}, susamiddhakulappajā;
::

::gathalast
Dhanañjānī ca khemā ca, ahampi ca tayo janā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārāmaṃ sukataṃ katvā, sabbāvayavamaṇḍitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhappamukhasaṅghassa, niyyādetvā samoditā.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha {pb:M:2.0188} yatthūpapajjāmi, tassa kammassa vāhasā;
::

::gathalast
Devesu aggataṃ pattā, manussesu tatheva ca.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappamhi, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko {pb:T:2.0255} mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
::

::gathalast
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāsuṃ satta dhītaro, rājakaññā sukhedhitā {note:sukhethitā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, brahmacariyaṃ cariṃsu tā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāsaṃ sahāyikā hutvā, sīlesu susamāhitā;
::

::gathalast
Datvā dānāni sakkaccaṃ, agāreva vataṃ {note:agāreva vattaṃ (syā.)} cariṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsūpagā ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ {note:yāmasaggaṃ (syā.)}, tatohaṃ tusitaṃ gatā;
::

::gathalast
Tato ca nimmānaratiṃ, vasavattipuraṃ tato.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha yatthūpapajjāmi, puññakammasamohitā;
::

::gathalast
Tattha tattheva rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:P:2.0513} cutā manussatte, rājūnaṃ cakkavattinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇḍalīnañca rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sampattimanubhotvāna, devesu mānusesu ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sukhitā hutvā, nekajātīsu saṃsariṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So hetu ca so pabhavo, tammūlaṃ sāsane khamaṃ {note:tammūlaṃ sā ca sāsane khanti (sī. pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Paṭhamaṃ taṃ samodhānaṃ, taṃ dhammaratāya nibbānaṃ {note:nibbutaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0181} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:T:2.0256} vata me āsi, mama buddhassa {note:buddhaseṭṭhassa (sī. syā. ka.)} santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:2.0189} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ sumedhā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Sumedhātheriyāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Mekhalādāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siddhatthassa bhagavato, thūpakārāpikā ahuṃ {note:thūpakāra makāsahaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Mekhalikā mayā dinnā, navakammāya satthuno.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Niṭṭhite ca mahāthūpe, mekhalaṃ punadāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lokanāthassa munino, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ mekhalamadaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, thūpakārassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
24\.

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:P:2.0514} vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0257} sudaṃ mekhalādāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mekhalādāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Maṇḍapadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koṇāgamanabuddhassa{pb:V:2.0182}, maṇḍapo kārito mayā;
::

::gathalast
Dhuvaṃ ticīvaraṃdāsiṃ {note:thūpañca pavaramadaṃ (syā.), dhuvañca cīvaraṃ adaṃ (pī.)}, buddhassa lokabandhuno.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ janapadaṃ yāmi, nigame rājadhāniyo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha pūjito homi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
29\.

::

::hangnum

::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ maṇḍapadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Maṇḍapadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Saṅkamanatthātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipassissa bhagavato {note:koṇḍaññassa bhagavato (syā. pī.)}, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Rathiyaṃ paṭipannassa, tārayantassa pāṇino.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gharato {pb:T:2.0258} nikkhamitvāna, avakujjā nipajjahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anukampako lokanātho, sirasi {note:sīsante (sī. ka.)} akkamī mama {note:tadā (syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkamitvāna sirasi {note:sambuddho (ka.)}, agamā lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Tena cittappasādena, tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.

::gatha1

Itthaṃ sudaṃ saṅkamanatthā {note:saṅkamanadā (syā.)} bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Saṅkamanatthātheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Naḷamālikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre{pb:V:2.0183}, ahosiṃ kinnarī tadā;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasannacittā sumanā, vedajātā katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Naḷamālaṃ gahetvāna, sayambhuṃ abhipūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:2.0191} kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā kinnarīdehaṃ, agacchiṃ tidasaṃ gatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chattiṃsadevarājūnaṃ{pb:T:2.0259}, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
::

::gatha2
Dasannaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṃvejetvāna me cittaṃ {note:vedayitvāna kusalaṃ (syā.), saṃvedayitvā kusalaṃ (pī.)}, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā {note:bhavā saṃghātitā mama (ka.)};
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
42\.

::gatha1

#### 6. Ekapiṇḍapātadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, bandhumā nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Tassa rañño ahuṃ bhariyā, ekajjhaṃ cārayāmahaṃ {note:ekaccaṃ vādayāmahaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rahogatā {pb:T:2.0260}{pb:V:2.0184} nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
‘Ādāya gamanīyañhi, kusalaṃ natthi me kataṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mahābhitāpaṃ {pb:P:2.0516} kaṭukaṃ, ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nirayaṃ nūna gacchāmi, ettha me natthi saṃsayo’.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājānaṃ upasaṅkamma, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘Ekaṃ me samaṇaṃ dehi, bhojayissāmi khattiya’.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adāsi me mahārājā, samaṇaṃ bhāvitindriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa pattaṃ gahetvāna, paramannena pūrayiṃ {note:tappayiṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pūrayitvā {pb:M:2.0192} paramannaṃ, gandhālepaṃ akāsahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jālena pidahitvāna, vatthayugena {note:pītacoḷena (syā.), mahānelena (pī.)} chādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārammaṇaṃ mamaṃ etaṃ, sarāmi yāvajīvihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṃsānaṃ devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manasā patthitaṃ mayhaṃ, nibbattati yathicchitaṃ {note:yaticchakaṃ (syā.), yadicchakaṃ (pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīsānaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ocitattāva {note:upacitattā (syā.)} hutvāna, saṃsarāmi bhavesvahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbabandhanamuttāhaṃ, apetā me upādikā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ {pb:T:2.0261} nābhijānāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ ekapiṇḍapātadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Ekapiṇḍapātadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piṇḍacāraṃ {pb:V:2.0185} carantassa, tissanāmassa satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ paggayha, buddhaseṭṭhassa dāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā {pb:P:2.0517} sambuddho, tisso lokagganāyako;
::

::gathalast
Vīthiyā saṇṭhito satthā, akā me anumodanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ {pb:M:2.0193} datvāna, tāvatiṃsaṃ gamissasi;
::

::gathalast
Chattiṃsadevarājūnaṃ, mahesittaṃ karissasi.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paññāsaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittaṃ karissasi;
::

::gathalast
Manasā patthitaṃ sabbaṃ, paṭilacchasi sabbadā.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sampattiṃ {pb:T:2.0262} anubhotvāna, pabbajissasikiñcanā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissasināsavā’.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, tisso lokagganāyako;
::

::gathalast
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī vīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sudinnaṃ me dānavaraṃ {note:sudinnameva me dānaṃ (syā.)}, suyiṭṭhā yāgasampadā;
::

::gathalast
Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ datvāna, pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 8. Sattuppalamālikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:V:2.0186} aruṇavatiyā, aruṇo nāma {note:aruṇavā nāma (sī. pī.)} ttiyo;
::

::gathalast
Tassa rañño ahuṃ bhariyā, vāritaṃ vārayāmahaṃ {note:cārikaṃ cārayāmahaṃ (sī.), na gulaṃ pādayāmahaṃ (syā.), na mālaṃ pādayāmahaṃ (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattamālaṃ {pb:T:2.0263} gahetvāna, uppalā devagandhikā;
::

::gathalast
Nisajja pāsādavare, evaṃ cintesi tāvade.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Varaṃ me buddhaseṭṭhassa, ñāṇamhi abhiropitaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambuddhaṃ {pb:P:2.0518} paṭimānentī, dvārāsanne nisīdahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘Yadā ehiti sambuddho, pūjayissaṃ mahāmuniṃ’.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kakudho vilasantova, migarājāva kesarī;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghena sahito, āgacchi vīthiyā jino.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhassa raṃsiṃ disvāna, haṭṭhā saṃviggamānasā;
::

::gathalast
Dvāraṃ avāpuritvāna {note:apāpuṇitvā (syā.)}, buddhaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satta uppalapupphāni, parikiṇṇāni {note:suvitthiṇṇāni (syā.)} ambare;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
78\.

#### 10. Udakadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
116\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deyyadhammo ca me natthi, puññakkhette anuttare;
::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::hangnum
123\.

::

::gathalast

124\.

‘‘Kadāci nīyamānāya, ñātisaṅghena me tadā;

::gathalast

::hangnum
125\.

::gatha1
‘‘Uṇhaṃ vā pariḷāho vā, sarīre me na vijjati;
::

::gathalast

126\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Visuddhamanasā {pb:P:2.0522} ajja, apetamanapāpikā;

::gathalast

::centre
Sumedhāvaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sumedhā mekhalādāyī, maṇḍapaṃ saṅkamaṃ dadā;
::

::gathalast
Naḷamālī piṇḍadadā, kaṭacchu uppalappadā.
::

::gatha1
Dīpadā dakadā ceva, gāthāyo gaṇitā iha;
::

::gathalast
Ekagāthāsatañceva, tiṃsati ca taduttari {note:sattarasaṃ taduttari (syā.), sattādasa taduttariṃ (pī.)}.
