### 2. Ekūposathikavaggo

#### 1. Ekūposathikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare {pb:T:2.0270}{pb:M:2.0199}{pb:V:2.0191} bandhumatiyā, bandhumā nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Divase puṇṇamāya so, upavasi uposathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ tena samayena, kumbhadāsī ahaṃ tahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvā sarājakaṃ senaṃ, evāhaṃ cintayiṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘Rājāpi rajjaṃ chaḍḍetvā, upavasi uposathaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saphalaṃ nūna taṃ kammaṃ, janakāyo pamodito’.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yoniso {pb:P:2.0523} paccavekkhitvā, duggaccañca {note:duggatiñca (syā.)} daliddataṃ {note:daḷiddataṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Mānasaṃ sampahaṃsitvā, upavasiṃ uposathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ uposathaṃ katvā, sammāsambuddhasāsane;
::

::gathalast
Tena kammena sukatena, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, ubbhayojanamuggataṃ {note:uddhaṃ yojanamuggataṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ, mahāsanasubhūsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accharā satasahassā, upatiṭṭhanti maṃ sadā;
::

::gathalast
Aññe deve atikkamma, atirocāmi sabbadā.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catusaṭṭhi devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṭṭhi cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇā {pb:T:2.0271} hutvāna, bhavesu saṃsarāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha pavarā homi, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, rathayānañca sīvikaṃ {note:kevalaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Soṇṇamayaṃ rūpimayaṃ, athopi phalikāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lohitaṅgamayañceva, sabbaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koseyyakambaliyāni{pb:V:2.0192}, khomakappāsikāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Mahagghāni ca vatthāni, sabbaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annaṃ {pb:M:2.0200} pānaṃ khādanīyaṃ, vatthasenāsanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Varagandhañca mālañca, cuṇṇakañca vilepanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kūṭāgārañca pāsādaṃ, maṇḍapaṃ hammiyaṃ guhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassāhaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito {pb:P:2.0524} kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:T:2.0272} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
21\.

::gatha1

#### 4. Ekāsanadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
41\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paññattamāsanamidaṃ, tavatthāya mahāmuni;

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nisīdi tattha samaṇo, sudanto suddhamānaso;

::gatha1

48\.

::gatha1

#### 5. Pañcadīpadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum

64\.

67\.

#### 7. Mahāpajāpatigotamītherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā jinassa mātucchā, mahāgotami bhikkhunī;

103\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
104\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Upanāmesi nāthassa, ānando buddhacodito.
::

::hangnum
278\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇinā tāni paggayha, avoca isisattamo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
279\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
280\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gathalast

::hangnum

::hangnum
284\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
285\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
286\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
287\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
288\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Bhāvetvā sattabojjhaṅge, dukkhassantaṃ karissatha’’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ mahāpajāpatigotamī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Mahāpajāpatigotamītheriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Khemātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
289\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
290\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ {pb:T:2.0301}{pb:V:2.0213} haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ {note:ahu (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Nānāratanapajjote, mahāsukhasamappitā.

::hangnum
291\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upetvā {pb:P:2.0544} taṃ mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
292\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
293\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
294\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, puno tassa mahesino;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
295\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
296\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
362\.

::gatha1
‘‘‘Namo te sabbadassāvī, namo te karuṇākara;
::

::gathalast
Namo te tiṇṇasaṃsāra, namo te amataṃ dada.
::

::hangnum
363\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Diṭṭhigahanapakkhandā {note:… pakkhantā (sī. syā.)}, kāmarāgavimohitā;
::

::gathalast
Tayā sammā upāyena, vinītā vinaye ratā.
::

::hangnum
364\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Adassanena vibhogā {note:vibbhogā (sī.), vihitā (syā.)}, tādisānaṃ mahesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anubhonti mahādukkhaṃ, sattā saṃsārasāgare.
::

::hangnum
365\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yadāhaṃ lokasaraṇaṃ, araṇaṃ araṇantaguṃ {note:maraṇantagaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Nāddasāmi adūraṭṭhaṃ, desayāmi {note:desessāmi (syā.)} tamaccayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
366\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mahāhitaṃ {pb:M:2.0228} varadadaṃ, ahitoti visaṅkitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
367\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:P:2.0550} madhuranigghoso, mahākāruṇiko jino;
::

::gathalast
Avoca tiṭṭha khemeti, siñcanto amatena maṃ.
::

::hangnum
368\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā paṇamya sirasā, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
369\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aho {pb:T:2.0309} sammā upāyo te, cintitoyamarindama;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
370\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yadi te ruccate rāja {note:rājā (syā.)}, sāsane tassa tādino;
::

::gathalast

::centre
Dutiyaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

::hangnum
371\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
372\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
373\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
374\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
375\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
376\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
377\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
378\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
379\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::gatha1

Itthaṃ sudaṃ khemā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Khemātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Uppalavaṇṇātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
384\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhikkhunī uppalavaṇṇā, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gatā;
::

::gathalast
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
385\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nitthiṇṇā {pb:V:2.0220} jātisaṃsāraṃ {note:jātisaṃsārā (pī.)}, pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbadukkhaṃ mayā khīṇaṃ, ārocemi mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
386\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yāvatā {pb:T:2.0311} parisā atthi, pasannā jinasāsane;
::

::gathalast
Yassā ca meparādhotthi, khamantu jinasammukhā.
::

::hangnum
387\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Saṃsāre saṃsarantiyā {note:saṃsarantā me (syā.)}, khalitaṃ me sace bhave;
::

::gathalast
Ārocemi mahāvīra, aparādhaṃ khamassu taṃ {note:me (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
388\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Iddhiñcāpi nidassehi, mama sāsanakārike;
::

::gathalast
Catasso parisā ajja, kaṅkhaṃ chindāhi yāvatā.
::

::hangnum
389\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dhītā tuyhaṃ mahāvīra, paññavanta jutindhara;
::

::gathalast
Bahuñca dukkaraṃ kammaṃ, kataṃ me atidukkaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
390\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Uppalasseva {pb:M:2.0230} me vaṇṇo, nāmenuppalanāmikā;
::

::gathalast
Sāvikā te mahāvīra, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma.
::

::hangnum
391\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Rāhulo ca ahañceva, nekajātisate bahū;
::

::gathalast
Ekasmiṃ sambhave jātā, samānachandamānasā.
::

::hangnum
392\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Nibbatti ekato hoti, jātiyāpi ca ekato {note:jātīsu bahuso mama (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pacchime bhave sampatte, ubhopi nānāsambhavā.
::

::hangnum
393\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Putto ca rāhulo nāma, dhītā uppalasavhayā;
::

::gathalast
Passa vīra mamaṃ iddhiṃ, balaṃ dassemi satthuno.
::

::hangnum
394\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mahāsamudde {pb:P:2.0552} caturo, pakkhipi hatthapātiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Telaṃ hatthagatañceva, khiḍḍo {note:vejjo (sī. pī.)} komārako yathā.
::

::hangnum
395\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ubbattayitvā pathaviṃ, pakkhipi hatthapātiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
396\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
397\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
398\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dhītāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa, nāmenuppalasavhayā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
399\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

400\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
448\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ, saṃsaritvā bhavābhave;
::

::gathalast
Tavatthāya mahāvīra, pariccattañca jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
449\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:P:2.0556} bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ, sampattī ca bahubbidhā;
::

::gathalast
Pacchime bhave sampatte, jātā sāvatthiyaṃ pure.
::

::hangnum
450\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahādhanaseṭṭhikule, sukhite sajjite tathā;
::

::gathalast
Nānāratanapajjote, sabbakāmasamiddhine.
::

::hangnum
451\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkatā pūjitā ceva, mānitāpacitā tathā;
::

::gathalast
Rūpasīrimanuppattā {note:rūpasobhaggasampannā (sī.)}, kulesu atisakkatā {note:abhisammatā (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
452\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atīva patthitā cāsiṃ, rūpabhogasirīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Patthitā seṭṭhiputtehi, anekehi satehipi.
::

::hangnum
453\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Agāraṃ pajahitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, catusaccamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
454\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddhiyā {pb:M:2.0235} abhinimmitvā, caturassaṃ rathaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa pāde vandissaṃ, lokanāthassa tādino.
::

::hangnum
455\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Supupphitaggaṃ {pb:V:2.0225} upagamma pādapaṃ {note:bhikkhunī (sī. pī. ka.) therīgā. 230}, ekā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi sālamūle;
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:T:2.0318} cāpi te dutiyo atthi koci {note:na catthi te dutiyā vaṇṇadhātu (sī. pī. ka.)}, bāle na tvaṃ bhāyasi dhuttakānaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
456\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sataṃ sahassānipi dhuttakānaṃ {note:sahassānampi dhuttakānaṃ (pī.) therīgā. 231}, samāgatā edisakā bhaveyyuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lomaṃ na iñje na sampavedhe, kiṃ me tuvaṃ māra karissaseko {note:na māra bhāyāmi tavekikāpi (sī. ka.) … tamekikāsiṃ (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
457\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Esā antaradhāyāmi, kucchiṃ vā pavisāmi te;
::

::gathalast
Bhamukantarikāyampi, tiṭṭhantiṃ maṃ na dakkhasi.
::

::hangnum
458\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Cittasmiṃ vasībhūtāmhi, iddhipādā subhāvitā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbabandhanamuttāmhi, na taṃ bhāyāmi āvuso.
::

::hangnum
459\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sattisūlūpamā kāmā, khandhāsaṃ adhikuṭṭanā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ tvaṃ kāmaratiṃ brūsi, aratī dāni sā mama.
::

::hangnum
460\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sabbattha {pb:P:2.0557} vihatā nandī, tamokhandho padālito;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ jānāhi pāpima, nihato tvamasi antaka’.
::

::hangnum
461\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jino tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggā iddhimatīnanti, parisāsu vināyako.
::

::hangnum
462\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
::

::hangnum
463\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
::

::hangnum
464\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cīvaraṃ {pb:T:2.0319}{pb:M:2.0236} piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khaṇena upanāmenti, sahassāni samantato.
::

::hangnum
465\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā;
::

::hangnum
466\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
467\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Uppalavaṇṇātheriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Paṭācārātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
468\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:V:2.0226} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
469\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānāratanapajjote, mahāsukhasamappitā.
::

::hangnum
470\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato jātapasādāhaṃ, upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
471\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato vinayadhārīnaṃ, aggaṃ vaṇṇesi nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhuniṃ lajjiniṃ tādiṃ, kappākappavisāradaṃ.
::

::hangnum
472\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:T:2.0320} muditacittāhaṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhikaṅkhinī;
::

::gathalast
Nimantetvā dasabalaṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
473\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhojayitvāna sattāhaṃ, daditvāva ticīvaraṃ {note:daditvā pattacīvaraṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Nipacca sirasā pāde, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
::

::hangnum
474\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yā tayā vaṇṇitā vīra, ito aṭṭhamake muni;
::

::gathalast
Tādisāhaṃ bhavissāmi, yadi sijjhati nāyaka’.
::

::hangnum
475\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:P:2.0558} avoca maṃ satthā, ‘bhadde mā bhāyi assasa;
::

::gathalast
Anāgatamhi addhāne, lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
476\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito {pb:M:2.0237} kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
477\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
::

::gathalast
Paṭācārāti nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
::

::hangnum
478\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ muditā {note:pamudī (ka.)} hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mettacittā paricariṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
479\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
480\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
481\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko {pb:V:2.0227} mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
::

::gathalast
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
::

::hangnum
482\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāsiṃ {pb:T:2.0321} tatiyā dhītā, bhikkhunī iti vissutā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
483\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anujāni na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
::

::hangnum
484\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā sattadhītaro.
::

::hangnum
485\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇī samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā.
::

::hangnum
486\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ uppalavaṇṇā ca, khemā bhaddā ca bhikkhunī;
::

::gathalast
Kisāgotamī dhammadinnā, visākhā hoti sattamī.
::

::hangnum
487\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tehi kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
488\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
::

::hangnum
489\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā {pb:M:2.0238} ca yobbanūpetā, vitakkavasagā ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Naraṃ jārapatiṃ disvā, tena saddhiṃ agacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
490\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekaputtapasūtāhaṃ{pb:P:2.0559}, dutiyo kucchiyā mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadāhaṃ mātāpitaro, okkhāmīti {note:ikkhāmīti (syā.), dakkhāmīti (sī.)} sunicchitā.
::

::hangnum
491\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nārocesiṃ patiṃ mayhaṃ, tadā tamhi pavāsite;
::

::gathalast
Ekikā niggatā gehā, gantuṃ sāvatthimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
492\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:T:2.0322} me sāmi āgantvā, sambhāvesi pathe mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadā me kammajā vātā, uppannā atidāruṇā.
::

::hangnum
493\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhito ca mahāmegho, pasūtisamaye mama;
::

::gathalast
Dabbatthāya tadā gantvā, sāmi sappena mārito.
::

::hangnum
494\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā vijātadukkhena, anāthā kapaṇā ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kunnadiṃ pūritaṃ disvā, gacchantī sakulālayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
495\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bālaṃ {pb:V:2.0228} ādāya atariṃ, pārakūle ca ekakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāyetvā {note:pāyetvā (syā.), pātetvā (ka.)} bālakaṃ puttaṃ, itaraṃ taraṇāyahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
496\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nivattā ukkuso hāsi, taruṇaṃ vilapantakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Itarañca vahī soto, sāhaṃ sokasamappitā.
::

::hangnum
497\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvatthinagaraṃ gantvā, assosiṃ sajane mate;
::

::gathalast
Tadā avocaṃ sokaṭṭā, mahāsokasamappitā.
::

::hangnum
498\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho puttā kālaṅkatā, panthe mayhaṃ patī mato;
::

::gathalast
Mātā pitā ca bhātā ca, ekacitamhi ḍayhare.
::

::hangnum
499\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā kisā ca paṇḍu ca, anāthā dīnamānasā;
::

::gathalast
Ito tato bhamantīhaṃ {note:gacchantīhaṃ (syā.), gamentīhaṃ (ka.)}, addasaṃ narasārathiṃ.
::

::hangnum
500\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato avoca maṃ satthā, ‘putte mā soci assasa;
::

::gathalast
Attānaṃ te gavesassu, kiṃ niratthaṃ vihaññasi.
::

::hangnum
501\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na santi puttā tāṇāya, na ñātī napi bandhavā;
::

::gathalast
Antakenādhipannassa, natthi ñātīsu tāṇatā’.
::

::hangnum
502\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:T:2.0323}{pb:M:2.0239} sutvā munino vākyaṃ, paṭhamaṃ phalamajjhagaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pabbajitvāna naciraṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
503\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddhīsu {pb:P:2.0560} ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
::

::gathalast
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
::

::hangnum
504\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
::

::hangnum
505\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatohaṃ vinayaṃ sabbaṃ, santike sabbadassino;
::

::gathalast
Uggahiṃ sabbavitthāraṃ, byāhariñca yathātathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
506\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggā vinayadhārīnaṃ, paṭācārāva ekikā.
::

::hangnum
507\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
::

::hangnum
508\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
::

::hangnum
509\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0229} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
510\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
511\.

::gatha1

::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0324} sudaṃ paṭācārā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Paṭācārātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Ekūposathikavaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Ekūposathikā ceva, saḷalā cātha modakā;
::

::gathalast
Ekāsanā pañcadīpā, naḷamālī ca gotamī.
::

::gatha1
Khemā uppalavaṇṇā ca, paṭācārā ca bhikkhunī;
::

::gathalast
Gāthā satāni pañceva, nava cāpi taduttari.
::

### 3. Kuṇḍalakesīvaggo

#### 1. Kuṇḍalakesātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0325}{pb:M:2.0240}{pb:V:2.0230} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānāratanapajjote, mahāsukhasamappitā.

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upetvā {pb:P:2.0561} taṃ mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato jātappasādāhaṃ, upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā mahākāruṇiko, padumuttaranāmako;
::

::gathalast
Khippābhiññānamagganti, ṭhapesi bhikkhuniṃ subhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, dānaṃ datvā mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Nipacca sirasā pāde, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anumodi mahāvīro, ‘bhadde yaṃ tebhipatthitaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
9\.

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:2.0326} kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;

::gatha1

::hangnum
11\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha yatthūpapajjāmi, tassa kammassa vāhasā;

::gathalast

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:2.0231} cutā manussesu, rājūnaṃ cakkavattinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maṇḍalīnañca rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sampattiṃ {pb:M:2.0241} anubhotvāna, devesu mānusesu ca;

::gathalast

::gatha1

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Coraṃ vadhatthaṃ nīyantaṃ, disvā rattā tahiṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pitā me taṃ sahassena, mocayitvā vadhā tato.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adāsi tassa maṃ tāto, viditvāna manaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Tassāhamāsiṃ visaṭṭhā, atīva dayitā hitā.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So me bhūsanalobhena, balimajjhāsayo {note:khalitajjhāsayo (sī.), baliṃ paccāharaṃ (syā.), mālapacchāhataṃ (pī.)} diso;
::

::gathalast
Corappapātaṃ netvāna, pabbataṃ cetayī vadhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ {pb:M:2.0242}{pb:V:2.0232} paṇamitvāna, sattukaṃ sukatañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhantī attano pāṇaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Idaṃ suvaṇṇakeyūraṃ, muttā veḷuriyā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ harassu {note:varassu (ka.)} bhaddante, mañca dāsīti sāvaya’.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Oropayassu kalyāṇī, mā bāḷhaṃ paridevasi;
::

::gathalast
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, ahantvā dhanamābhataṃ’.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yato {pb:T:2.0328} sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā’.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Ehi taṃ upagūhissaṃ, katvāna taṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na ca dāni puno atthi {note:taṃ vandāmi puna natthi (syā.)}, mama tuyhañca saṅgamo.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Itthīpi paṇḍitā hoti, tattha tattha vicakkhaṇā.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Itthīpi paṇḍitā hoti, lahuṃ atthavicintikā.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Lahuñca {pb:P:2.0563} vata khippañca, nikaṭṭhe {note:nekatthe (sī. syā.)} samacetayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Migaṃ uṇṇā yathā evaṃ {note:cittapuṇṇāya tāneva (syā.), migaṃ puṇṇāya teneva (pī.)}, tadāhaṃ sattukaṃ vadhiṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
::

::gathalast
So haññate mandamati, corova girigabbhare.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
::

::gathalast
Muccate sattusambādhā, tadāhaṃ sattukā yathā’.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ pātayitvāna, giriduggamhi sattukaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Santikaṃ setavatthānaṃ, upetvā pabbajiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṇḍāsena ca kese me, luñcitvā sabbaso tadā;
::

::gathalast
Pabbajitvāna samayaṃ, ācikkhiṃsu nirantaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato taṃ uggahetvāhaṃ, nisīditvāna ekikā;
::

::gathalast
Samayaṃ taṃ vicintesiṃ, suvāno mānusaṃ karaṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chinnaṃ {pb:T:2.0329}{pb:M:2.0243} gayha samīpe me, pātayitvā apakkami;
::

::gathalast
Disvā nimittamalabhiṃ, hatthaṃ taṃ puḷavākulaṃ.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:2.0233} uṭṭhāya saṃviggā, apucchiṃ sahadhammike;
::

::gathalast
Te avocuṃ vijānanti, taṃ atthaṃ sakyabhikkhavo.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāhaṃ tamatthaṃ pucchissaṃ, upetvā buddhasāvake;
::

::gathalast
Te mamādāya gacchiṃsu, buddhaseṭṭhassa santikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So me dhammamadesesi, khandhāyatanadhātuyo;
::

::gathalast
Asubhāniccadukkhāti, anattāti ca nāyako.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ, dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato viññātasaddhammā, pabbajjaṃ upasampadaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āyācito tadā āha, ‘ehi bhadde’ti nāyako;
::

::gathalast
Tadāhaṃ upasampannā, parittaṃ toyamaddasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pādapakkhālanenāhaṃ{pb:P:2.0564}, ñatvā saudayabbayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathā sabbepi saṅkhāre, īdisaṃ cintayiṃ {note:saṅkhārā, iti saṃcintayiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} tadā.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato cittaṃ vimucci me, anupādāya sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Khippābhiññānamaggaṃ me, tadā paññāpayī jino.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
::

::gathalast
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pariciṇṇo {pb:T:2.0330} mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa sāsane.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:M:2.0244} jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:V:2.0234} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhaddākuṇḍalakesā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Kuṇḍalakesātheriyāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Kisāgotamītherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ {pb:T:2.0331} haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā aññatare kule;
::

::gathalast
Upetvā taṃ naravaraṃ, saraṇaṃ samupāgamiṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammañca tassa assosiṃ, catusaccūpasañhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Madhuraṃ paramassādaṃ, vaṭṭasantisukhāvahaṃ {note:cittasanti … (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā ca bhikkhuniṃ vīro, lūkhacīvaradhāriniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhapento etadaggamhi, vaṇṇayī purisuttamo.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Janetvānappakaṃ {pb:P:2.0565} pītiṃ, sutvā bhikkhuniyā guṇe;
::

::gathalast
Kāraṃ katvāna buddhassa, yathāsatti yathābalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nipacca munivaraṃ taṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadānumodi sambuddho, ṭhānalābhāya nāyako.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
::

::gathalast
Kisāgotamī {note:gotamī nāma (sī. ka.)} nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:M:2.0245} sutvā muditā hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mettacittā paricariṃ, paccayehi vināyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imamhi {pb:V:2.0235} bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko {pb:T:2.0332} mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
::

::gathalast
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcamī tassa dhītāsiṃ, dhammā nāmena vissutā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anujāni na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā satta dhītaro.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇī samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khemā uppalavaṇṇā ca, paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca dhammadinnā ca, visākhā hoti sattamī.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tehi kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Duggate adhane naṭṭhe {note:nīce (syā.), niddhe (pī.)}, gatā ca sadhanaṃ kulaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patiṃ ṭhapetvā sesā me, dessanti adhanā iti;
::

::gathalast
Yadā ca pasūtā {note:sasutā (sī. pī.)} āsiṃ, sabbesaṃ dayitā tadā.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā {pb:P:2.0566} so taruṇo bhaddo {note:putto (sī. syā.)}, komalako {note:komārako (syā.), komalaṅgo (sī. pī.)} sukhedhito;
::

::gathalast
Sapāṇamiva kanto me, tadā yamavasaṃ gato.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sokaṭṭā {pb:T:2.0333} dīnavadanā{pb:M:2.0246}, assunettā rudammukhā;
::

::gathalast
Mataṃ kuṇapamādāya, vilapantī gamāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā ekena sandiṭṭhā, upetvābhisakkuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avocaṃ dehi bhesajjaṃ, puttasañjīvananti bho.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na vijjante matā yasmiṃ, gehe siddhatthakaṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Āharāti jino āha, vinayopāyakovido.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:V:2.0236} gamitvā sāvatthiṃ, na labhiṃ tādisaṃ gharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kuto siddhatthakaṃ tasmā, tato laddhā satiṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṇapaṃ chaḍḍayitvāna, upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dūratova mamaṃ disvā, avoca madhurassaro.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yo ca vassasataṃ jīve, apassaṃ udayabbayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekāhaṃ jīvitaṃ seyyo, passato udayabbayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Na gāmadhammo nigamassa dhammo, na cāpiyaṃ ekakulassa dhammo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbassa lokassa sadevakassa, eseva dhammo yadidaṃ aniccatā’.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāhaṃ sutvānimā {note:sahasutvānimā (ka.)} gāthā, dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato viññātasaddhammā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathā pabbajitā santī, yuñjantī jinasāsane;
::

::gathalast
Na cireneva kālena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddhīsu {pb:T:2.0334} ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
::

::gathalast
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassatthāya {pb:M:2.0247}{pb:P:2.0567} pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkārakūṭā āhitvā, susānā rathiyāpi ca;
::

::gathalast
Tato saṅghāṭikaṃ katvā, lūkhaṃ dhāremi cīvaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, lūkhacīvaradhāraṇe;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi, parisāsu vināyako.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā {pb:V:2.0237} jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ {pb:T:2.0335} sudaṃ kisāgotamī bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Kisāgotamītheriyāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Dhammadinnātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, kule aññatare ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parakammakārī āsiṃ, nipakā sīlasaṃvutā.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, sujāto aggasāvako;
::

::gathalast
Vihārā abhinikkhamma, piṇḍapātāya {note:pattamādāya (ka.)} gacchati.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ghaṭaṃ gahetvā gacchantī, tadā udakahārikā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ disvā adadaṃ pūpaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā tattheva, nisinno paribhuñji so;
::

::gathalast
Tato netvāna taṃ gehaṃ, adāsiṃ tassa bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:2.0248} me ayyako tuṭṭho, akarī suṇisaṃ sakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sassuyā saha gantvāna, sambuddhaṃ abhivādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā so dhammakathikaṃ, bhikkhuniṃ parikittayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi, taṃ sutvā muditā ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nimantayitvā {pb:P:2.0568} sugataṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:T:2.0336} maṃ sugato āha, ghananinnādasussaro {note:ghananinnādasussare (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
‘Mamupaṭṭhānanirate, sasaṅghaparivesike.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Saddhammassavane {pb:V:2.0238} yutte, guṇavaddhitamānase;
::

::gathalast
Bhadde bhavassu muditā, lacchase paṇidhīphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammadinnāti nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ mahāmuniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mettacittā paricariṃ, paccayehi vināyakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

Buddhassa apakārena, duggandhā vadanena ca.
::

::hangnum
286\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puna kassapavīrassa, nidhāyantamhi cetiye;

#### 8. Yasodharātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast
Pabbhāramhi varekamhi, vasante naranāyake.

::hangnum
315\.
::

::gatha1

‘‘‘Samacittā {pb:V:2.0258} samakammā, samakārī bhavissati;

::gathalast

#### 9. Yasodharāpamukhadasabhikkhunīsahassaapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
412\.

413\.

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

415\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānaṃ sīlamayaṃ sabbaṃ, bhāvanā ca subhāvitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
416\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
417\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
418\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anekajātisaṃsāraṃ, bahuṃ puññampi no kataṃ;
::

::gathalast

419\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
420\.

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
421\.

422\.

::hangnum
461\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kappe {pb:T:2.0373} ca satasahasse, caturo ca asaṅkhiye;
::

::gathalast
Dīpaṅkaro mahāvīro, uppajji lokanāyako.
::

::hangnum
462\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paccantadesavisaye, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa āgamanaṃ maggaṃ, sodhenti tuṭṭhamānasā.
::

::hangnum
463\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tena {pb:P:2.0595} kālena so āsi, sumedho nāma brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Maggañca paṭiyādesi, āyato sabbadassino.
::

::hangnum
464\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tena kālena ahumha, sabbā brāhmaṇasambhavā;
::

::gathalast
Thalūdajāni pupphāni, āharimha samāgamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
465\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tasmiṃ so samaye buddho, dīpaṅkaro mahāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Viyākāsi mahāvīro, isimuggatamānasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
466\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Calatī ravatī puthavī, saṅkampati sadevake;
::

::gathalast
Tassa kammaṃ pakittente, isimuggatamānasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
467\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Devakaññā {pb:V:2.0265} manussā ca, mayañcāpi sadevakā;
::

::gathalast
Nānāpūjanīyaṃ bhaṇḍaṃ, pūjayitvāna patthayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
468\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tesaṃ buddho viyākāsi, jotidīpa sanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Ajja ye patthitā atthi, te bhavissanti sammukhā.
::

::hangnum
469\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, yaṃ no buddho viyākari;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ vācamanumodentā, evaṃkārī ahumha no.
::

::hangnum
470\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tassa kammassa sukatassa, tassa cittaṃ pasādayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devamānusikaṃ yoniṃ, anubhotvā asaṅkhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
471\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sukhadukkhenubhotvāna{pb:T:2.0374}, devesu mānusesu ca;
::

::gathalast
Pacchime bhave sampatte, jātāmha sākiye kule.
::

::hangnum
472\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Rūpavatī {pb:M:2.0277} bhogavatī, yasasīlavatī tato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṅgasampadā homa, kulesu abhisakkatā.
::

::hangnum
473\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Lābhaṃ silokaṃ sakkāraṃ, lokadhammasamāgamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cittañca dukkhitaṃ natthi, vasāma akutobhayā.
::

::hangnum
474\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Vuttañhetaṃ bhagavatā, rañño antepure tadā;
::

::gathalast
Khattiyānaṃ pure vīra {note:tāsaṃ (syā.)}, upakārañca niddisi.
::

::hangnum
475\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Upakārā ca yā nārī, yā ca nārī sukhe dukhe;
::

::gathalast
Atthakkhāyī ca yā nārī, yā ca nārīnukampikā.
::

::hangnum
476\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Dhammaṃ {pb:P:2.0596} care sucaritaṃ, na naṃ duccaritaṃ care;
::

::gathalast
Dhammacārī sukhaṃ seti, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
::

::hangnum
477\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Agāraṃ vijahitvāna, pabbajimhanagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, catusaccaṃ phusimha no.
::

::hangnum
478\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upanenti bahū amhe, sāgarasseva ūmiyo.
::

::hangnum
479\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā amhaṃ {note:mayhaṃ (syā.), amhākaṃ (ka.)}, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāma anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
480\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Svāgataṃ vata no āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
481\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:T:2.0375}{pb:V:2.0266} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
482\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ, sampattī ca bahubbidhā;
::

::gathalast
Visuddhabhāvaṃ sampattā, labhāma sabbasampadā.
::

::hangnum
483\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yā dadanti sakattānaṃ, puññatthāya mahesino;
::

::gathalast
Sahāyasampadā honti, nibbānapadamasaṅkhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
484\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parikkhīṇaṃ atītañca, paccuppannaṃ anāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakammampi no khīṇaṃ, pāde vandāma cakkhuma.
::

::hangnum
485\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbānāya {pb:M:2.0278} vadantīnaṃ, kiṃ vo vakkhāma uttari;
::

::gathalast
Santasaṅkhatadosañhi, pappotha {note:santasaṅkhatadoso yo, pajjotaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)} amataṃ padaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharāpamukhāni aṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Yasodharāpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kuṇḍalakesīvaggo tatiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kuṇḍalā gotamī ceva, dhammadinnā ca sakulā;
::

::gathalast
Varanandā ca soṇā ca, kāpilānī yasodharā.
::

::gatha1
Dasasahassabhikkhunī, aṭṭhārasasahassakā;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāsatāni cattāri, cha ca sattatimeva ca {note:aṭṭhasattatimeva ca (syā.)}.
::

### 4. Khattiyāvaggo

#### 1. Yasavatīpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassaapadānaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavā {pb:T:2.0376}{pb:M:2.0279}{pb:V:2.0267}{pb:P:2.0597} sabbe parikkhīṇā, bhavā santi vimocitā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavā ca no natthi, ārocema mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purimaṃ kusalaṃ kammaṃ {note:parikammañca kusalaṃ (syā.)}, yaṃ kiñci sādhupatthitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhapaccekabuddhānaṃ, sāvakānañca patthitaṃ {note:buddhānaṃ sāvakānañca (sī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uccanīcamayaṃ kammaṃ, bhikkhūnaṃ sādhupatthitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uccākulaparikammaṃ, katametaṃ mahāmune {note:katamhehi mahāmune (syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Teneva sukkamūlena, coditā kammasampadā;
::

::gathalast
Mānusikamatikkantā, jāyiṃsu khattiye kule.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uppatte ca kate kamme, jātiyā vāpi ekato;
::

::gathalast
Pacchime ekato jātā, khattiyā kulasambhavā.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpavatī bhogavatī, lābhasakkārapūjitā;
::

::gathalast
Antepure mahāvīra, devānaṃ viya nandane.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbinditvā agāramhā, pabbajimhanagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Katipāhaṃ upādāya, sabbā pattāmha nibbutiṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cīvaraṃ {pb:T:2.0377} piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upanenti bahū amhe, sadā sakkatapūjitā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā amhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāma anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata no āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā {pb:M:2.0280}{pb:V:2.0268} catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
::

::gathalast
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasavatīpamukhāni khattiyakaññābhikkhuniyo aṭṭhārasasahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Yasavatīpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Caturāsītibhikkhunīsahassaapadānaṃ

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni{pb:P:2.0598}, brāhmaññakulasambhavā {note:brāhmaṇakulasambhavā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sukhumālahatthapādā, pure tuyhaṃ mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vessasuddakule jātā, devā nāgā ca kinnarā;
::

::gathalast
Cātuddīpā bahū kaññā, pure tuyhaṃ mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāci pabbajitā atthi, sabbadassāvino {note:saccadassāvino (sī. pī.)} hū;
::

::gathalast
Devā ca kinnarā nāgā, phusissanti anāgate.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anubhotvā yasaṃ sabbaṃ, patvāna sabbasampadā;
::

::gathalast
Tumhaṃ {pb:T:2.0378} {note:tvayi (sī. pī.)} pasādaṃ paṭiladdhā, bujjhissanti anāgate.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amhe brāhmaṇadhītā tu, brāhmaññakulasambhavā;
::

::gathalast
Pekkhato no {note:lakkhaṇā ca (syā.)} mahāvīra, pāde vandāma cakkhuma.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upahatā bhavā sabbe, mūlataṇhā samūhatā;
::

::gathalast
Samucchinnā anusayā, puññasaṅkhāradālitā.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samādhigocarā sabbā, samāpattivasī katā;
::

::gathalast
Jhānena dhammaratiyā, viharissāma no sadā.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavanetti avijjā ca, saṅkhārāpi ca khepitā;
::

::gathalast
Sududdasaṃ padaṃ gantvā, anujānātha {note:anujānimha (syā. pī. ka.)} nāyaka.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upakārā mamaṃ tumhe, dīgharattaṃ katāvino;
::

::gathalast
Catunnaṃ saṃsayaṃ chetvā, sabbā gacchantu nibbutiṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanditvā {pb:M:2.0281}{pb:V:2.0269} munino pāde, katvā iddhivikubbanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāci dassenti ālokaṃ, andhakāramathāparā.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dassenti candasūriye, sāgarañca samacchakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sineruṃ paribhaṇḍañca, dassenti pārichattakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāvatiṃsañca bhavanaṃ, yāmaṃ dassenti iddhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Tusitaṃ nimmite deve, vasavattī mahissare.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brahmāno kāci dassenti, caṅkamañca mahārahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Brahmavaṇṇañca māpetvā, dhammaṃ desenti suññataṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nānāvikubbanaṃ katvā, iddhiṃ dassiya satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Dassayiṃsu {pb:T:2.0379} balaṃ sabbā, pāde vandiṃsu satthuno.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddhīsu {pb:P:2.0599} ca vasī homa, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
::

::gathalast
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homa mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāma, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇaṃ amhaṃ mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ, saṅgamaṃ no nidassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ amhaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ amhehi kataṃ kammaṃ, kusalaṃ sara taṃ mune;
::

::gathalast
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, puññānupacitāni no.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Puraṃ haṃsavatī nāma, sambuddhassa kulāsayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvārena haṃsavatiyā, gaṅgā sandati sabbadā;
::

::gathalast
Ubbaḷhā nadiyā bhikkhū, gamanaṃ na labhanti te.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Divasaṃ dve tayo ceva, sattāhaṃ māsikaṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Catumāsampi sampuṇṇaṃ, gamanaṃ na labhanti te.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā ahu sattasāro, jaṭilo nāma raṭṭhiko;
::

::gathalast
Oruddhe {note:oratīre (syā.)} bhikkhavo disvā, setuṃ gaṅgāya kārayi.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā {pb:T:2.0380}{pb:M:2.0282}{pb:V:2.0270} satasahassehi, setuṃ gaṅgāya kārayi;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghassa orime tīre, vihārañca akārayi.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Itthiyo purisā ceva, uccanīcakulāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Tassa setuṃ vihārañca {note:tesu setuvihāresu (sī.), tassa setū vihāre ca (pī.)}, samabhāgaṃ akaṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amhe aññe ca mānujā, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, nagare janapadesu ca.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Itthī pumā kumārā ca, bahū ceva kumārikā;
::

::gathalast
Setuno ca vihārassa, vālukā ākiriṃsu te.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīthiṃ {pb:P:2.0600} sammajjanaṃ katvā, kadalīpuṇṇaghaṭe dhaje;
::

::gathalast
Dhūpaṃ cuṇṇañca mālañca, kāraṃ katvāna satthuno.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Setuvihāre kāretvā, nimantetvā vināyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, sambodhiṃ abhipatthayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro mahāvīro, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anumodanīyaṃkāsi, jaṭilassa mahāmuni {note:katvā, viyākāsi mahāmuni (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Satasahassātikkante, kappo hessati bhaddako;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Kāci hatthaparikammaṃ, katāvī naranāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Anāgatamhi addhāne, sabbā hessanti sammukhā’.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Uppannā devabhavanaṃ, tuyhaṃ tā paricārikā.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbasukhaṃ {pb:T:2.0381} asaṅkhiyaṃ, mānusañca asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tuyhaṃ te paricārema, saṃsarimha bhavābhave.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, sukataṃ kammasampadaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhumālī manussānaṃ, atho devapure vare.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpabhogayase ceva, atho kittiñca sakkataṃ {note:kittisukhaṃ piyaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Labhāma satataṃ sabbaṃ, sukataṃ kammasampadaṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime {pb:M:2.0283} bhave sampatte, jātāmha brāhmaṇe kule;
::

::gathalast
Sukhumālahatthapādā, sakyaputtanivesane.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbakālampi {pb:V:2.0271} pathaviṃ, na passāma na laṅkataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cikkhallabhūmimasuciṃ {note:cikkhallaṃ bhūmiṃ gamanaṃ (syā.)}, na passāma mahāmune.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Agāraṃ vasante amhe, sakkāraṃ sabbakālikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upanenti sadā sabbaṃ, pubbakammaphalena no {note:pubbakammaphalaṃ tato (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Agāraṃ {pb:P:2.0601} pajahitvāna, pabbajitvānagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṃsārapathanitthiṇṇā, vītarāgā bhavāmase {note:natthi dāni punabbhavo (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upanenti sadā amhe, sahassāni tato tato.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā amhaṃ…pe… viharāma anāsavā.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:T:2.0382} vata no āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ caturāsītibrāhmaṇakaññābhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

::centre
Caturāsītibhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Uppaladāyikātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagare aruṇavatiyā, aruṇo nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Tassa rañño ahuṃ bhariyā, ekajjhaṃ cārayāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rahogatā nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
‘Kusalaṃ me kataṃ natthi, ādāya gamiyaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Mahābhitāpaṃ kaṭukaṃ, ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nirayaṃ nūna gacchāmi, ettha me natthi saṃsayo’.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evāhaṃ {pb:M:2.0284} cintayitvāna, pahaṃsetvāna mānasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rājānaṃ upagantvāna, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Itthī nāma mayaṃ deva, purisānittarā ahu {note:purisānugatā sadā (sī.), purisā na bhavāma no (syā.), purisānaṃ bharā mayaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃ me samaṇaṃ dehi, bhojayissāmi khattiya’.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adāsi {pb:V:2.0272} me tadā rājā, samaṇaṃ bhāvitindriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa pattaṃ gahetvāna, paramannena pūrayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pūretvā {pb:T:2.0383}{pb:P:2.0602} paramaṃ annaṃ, saha sugandhalepanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahācelena chāditvā, adāsiṃ tuṭṭhamānasā.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassadevarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sahassacakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ aññaṃ, tassa kammaphalaṃ tato.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uppalasseva me vaṇṇo, abhirūpā sudassanā;
::

::gathalast
Itthisabbaṅgasampannā, abhijātā jutindharā.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, ajāyiṃ sākiye kule;
::

::gathalast
Nārīsahassapāmokkhā, suddhodanasutassahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbinditvā agārehaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattamīrattisampattā {note:sattamiṃrattimapattā (sī. syā. pī.)}, catusaccamapāpuṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parimetuṃ na sakkomi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ mayhaṃ pūritaṃ kammaṃ, kusalaṃ sarase muni;
::

::gathalast
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, paricattaṃ bahuṃ mayā.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dve {pb:T:2.0384}{pb:M:2.0285} gatiyo pajānāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ucce kule pajāyāmi, mahāsāle {note:tayo sāla (ka.)} mahaddhane;
::

::gathalast
Aññe kule na jāyāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavābhave saṃsaritvā, sukkamūlena coditā;
::

::gathalast
Amanāpaṃ na passāmi, somanassakataṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddhīsu {pb:V:2.0273}{pb:P:2.0603} ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.

::

::gatha1
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::centre

#### 4. Siṅgālamātutherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Padumuttaro {pb:T:2.0385} nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātāmaccakule ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pitunā saha gantvāna, mahājanapurakkhatā;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbajitvāna {pb:M:2.0286} kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhe pasannā dhamme ca, saṅghe ca tibbagāravā;
::

::gathalast
Saddhammassavane yuttā, buddhadassanalālasā {note:buddhadassanasālayā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggaṃ saddhādhimuttānaṃ, assosiṃ bhikkhuniṃ tadā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayitvāna, tisso sikkhā apūrayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:2.0274} maṃ sugato āha, karuṇānugatāsayo;
::

::gatha2
‘Yassa saddhā tathāgate, acalā suppatiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Sīlañca {pb:P:2.0604} yassa kalyāṇaṃ, ariyakantaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Saṅghe pasādo yassatthi, ujubhūtañca dassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adaliddoti taṃ āhu, amoghaṃ tassa jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Tasmā saddhañca sīlañca, pasādaṃ dhammadassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anuyuñjetha {pb:T:2.0386} medhāvī, saraṃ buddhāna {note:buddhānusāsanaṃ (sī.), buddhānaṃ sāsanaṃ (syā.)} sāsanaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sutvāhaṃ pamuditā, apucchiṃ paṇidhiṃ mama;
::

::gatha2
Tadā anomo amito, byākarittha vināyako;
::

::gathalast
‘Buddhe pasannā kalyāṇī, lacchase taṃ supatthitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gathalast

94\.

114\.

#### 6. Abhirūpanandātherīapadānaṃ

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, vipassī nāma nāyako;

::gathalast

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ, iddhe phīte mahākule;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upagantvā mahāvīraṃ, vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīlesu saṃvutā hutvā, nibbute ca naruttame;
::

::gathalast
Dhātuthūpassa upari, soṇṇacchattamapūjayiṃ.

::hangnum
147\.

::gatha1
‘‘Muttacāgā sīlavatī, yāvajīvaṃ tato cutā;
::

233\.

::

::gathalast

::

::

::centre
Khattiyāvaggo catuttho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Khattiyā {pb:T:2.0402} brāhmaṇī ceva, tathā uppaladāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Siṅgālamātā sukkā ca, abhirūpā aḍḍhakāsikā.
::

::gatha1
Puṇṇā ca ambapālī ca, pesalāti ca tā dasa;
::

::gathalast
Gāthāyo dvisatānettha, dvicattālīsa cuttari.
::

Atha {pb:V:2.0286} vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sumedhā ekūposathā, kuṇḍalakesī khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sahassaṃ tisatā gāthā, sattatālīsa piṇḍitā.
::

::gatha1
Saha uddānagāthāhi, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi;
::

::gathalast
Sahassaṃ tisataṃ gāthā, sattapaññāsameva cāti.
::

::centre
Therikāpadānaṃ samattaṃ.
::

::centre
Apadānapāḷi samattā.
::
